### [1] [Automated LTL Specification Generation from Industrial Aerospace Requirements](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21715v1)
*Zhi Ma,Xiao Liang,Cheng Wen,Rui Chen,Bin Gu,Shengchao Qin,Cong Tian,Mengfei Yang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AeroReq2LTL使用LLM结合数据字典和模板语言，自动将自然语言需求转化为LTL属性，在真实数据集上达到85%精度和88%召回率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将自然语言需求转化为LTL属性是劳动密集且易错的过程，需要专业知识，现有工具在工业环境下因复杂术语和隐含结构而失败。

Method: 提出AeroReq2LTL框架，利用LLM，并引入数据字典规范化术语和模板语言显式化时序与逻辑结构。

Result: 在真实航空航天数据集上，生成LTL的精度为85%，召回率为88%，输出可直接用于验证工具。

Conclusion: AeroReq2LTL有效自动化了航空航天需求的LTL生成，提高了准确性和可用性。

中文摘要：在安全关键性航空航天软件的开发和验证中，线性时序逻辑（LTL）已被广泛用于规范从需求中导出的复杂系统属性。然而，工业实践中仍存在显著差距：将自然语言（NL）需求转化为正式的LTL属性是一个劳动密集型且容易出错的过程，需要航空航天控制工程和形式化方法方面的罕见专业知识。虽然最近的NL-to-LTL工具（如NL2SPEC、NL2TL、NL2LTL）能够自动化部分过程，但由于复杂的领域术语或隐含的时序和逻辑结构，它们在工业环境的真实需求文档上常常失败。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了AeroReq2LTL，一个使用大型语言模型（LLM）自动化航空航天需求LTL属性生成的框架，具有两个关键的工业创新：（i）一个数据字典，将技术术语规范化为精确的原子命题；（ii）一个基于模板的需求语言，在翻译之前使时序线索和逻辑关系显式化。在真实航空航天数据集上，AeroReq2LTL在LTL生成中实现了85%的精度和88%的召回率，其输出可直接被现有验证工具使用。

Original abstract: In the development and verification of safety-critical aero-space software, Linear Temporal Logic (LTL) has been widely used to specify complex system properties derived from requirements. However, a significant gap remains in industrial practice: translating natural language (NL) requirements into formal LTL properties is a labor-intensive and error-prone process that requires rare expertise in both aerospace control engineering and formal methods. While recent NL-to-LTL tools (e.g., NL2SPEC, NL2TL, NL2LTL) are capable of automating parts of this process, they often fail on real requirement documents in industrial settings, due to complex domain terminology or implicit temporal and logical structure. To address these challenges, we present AeroReq2LTL, a framework that automates LTL property generation for aerospace requirements using large language models (LLMs), with two key industrial innovations: (i) a data dictionary that normalizes technical jargon into precise atomic propositions; and (ii) a template-based requirement language that makes temporal cues and logical relations explicit before translation. On a real aerospace dataset, AeroReq2LTL achieves 85% precision and 88% recall in LTL generation, and its outputs can be directly consumed by existing verification tools.

</details>


### [2] [Proactive Detection of GUI Defects in Multi-Window Scenarios via Multimodal Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19081v1)
*Xinyao Zhang,Rui Wang,Jinhao Cui,Haotian Huang,Wei Xue,Wenhua Hu,Jianwen Xiang,Rui Hao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一个主动触发的端到端框架，利用多模态大语言模型和SoM对齐，在多窗口移动场景中检测GUI显示缺陷，实验表明其性能优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GUI缺陷检测方法被动且主要针对全屏界面，难以应对多窗口移动场景中因窗口变化和布局重排导致的显示缺陷。

Method: 构建端到端框架，主动触发分屏、折叠和窗口过渡状态，利用Set-of-Mark (SoM)对齐截图与控件元素，并结合多模态大语言模型和思维链提示进行缺陷检测、定位和解释。

Result: 多窗口设置使布局缺陷暴露增加，文本截断增长184%；应用级检测假阳性率10.00%，假阴性率11.11%；细粒度控件遮挡检测F1达87.2%，优于基线。

Conclusion: 该框架能有效检测多窗口移动场景中的GUI显示缺陷，且通过主动触发和细粒度对齐显著提升检测性能。

中文摘要：多窗口移动场景（如分屏和折叠模式）使GUI显示缺陷更可能出现，因为应用程序必须适应不断变化的窗口大小和动态布局重排。现有的检测技术有两个局限性：它们主要是被动的，仅在问题状态达到后分析截图，并且主要设计用于传统的全屏界面，在多窗口设置中效果较差。我们提出了一个端到端的框架，用于多窗口移动场景中的GUI显示缺陷检测。该框架在应用探索期间主动触发分屏、折叠和窗口过渡状态，使用标记集（SoM）将截图与控件级界面元素对齐，并利用多模态大语言模型和思维链提示来检测、定位和解释显示缺陷。我们还使用50个真实的Android应用构建了一个GUI显示缺陷基准。实验结果表明，多窗口设置显著增加了布局相关缺陷的暴露，文本截断比传统全屏设置增加了184%。在应用层面，我们的方法检测出40个有缺陷的应用，假阳性率为10.00%，假阴性率为11.11%，优于OwlEye和基于YOLO的基线。在细粒度层面，它在控件遮挡检测上取得了87.2%的最佳F1分数。

Original abstract: Multi-window mobile scenarios, such as split-screen and foldable modes, make GUI display defects more likely by forcing applications to adapt to changing window sizes and dynamic layout reflow. Existing detection techniques are limited in two ways: they are largely passive, analyzing screenshots only after problematic states have been reached, and they are mainly designed for conventional full-screen interfaces, making them less effective in multi-window settings.We propose an end-to-end framework for GUI display defect detection in multi-window mobile scenarios. The framework proactively triggers split-screen, foldable, and window-transition states during app exploration, uses Set-of-Mark (SoM) to align screenshots with widget-level interface elements, and leverages multimodal large language models with chain-of-thought prompting to detect, localize, and explain display defects. We also construct a benchmark of GUI display defects using 50 real-world Android applications.Experimental results show that multi-window settings substantially increase the exposure of layout-related defects, with text truncation increasing by 184% compared with conventional full-screen settings. At the application level, our method detects 40 defect-prone apps with a false positive rate of 10.00% and a false negative rate of 11.11%, outperforming OwlEye and YOLO-based baselines. At the fine-grained level, it achieves the best F1 score of 87.2% for widget occlusion detection.

</details>


### [3] [MUCOCO: Automated Consistency Testing of Code LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19086v1)
*Chua Jin Chou,Khant That Lwin,Ezekiel Soremekun*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出MUCOCO方法，通过语义保持变异分析自动检测代码LLM中的不一致行为，实验表明有效且优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试多为手工静态，不针对一致性，需要自动发现代码LLM不一致行为的方法。

Method: 采用语义保持变异分析，将程序转换为等价变异体，检测变异体与原始程序之间的输出不一致或测试失败。

Result: 在4个编码任务和7个LLM上评估，MUCOCO有效暴露不一致性，约15%输入触发不一致，优于TURBULENCE基线。

Conclusion: 代码LLM需要测试一致性属性，MUCOCO提供了一种自动测试方法。

中文摘要：代码大语言模型经常表现出不一致的程序行为。开发者通常使用基准测试来评估代码大语言模型，但大多数基准测试是手工制作的、静态的，且不针对一致性属性。在这项工作中，我们提出了一个科学问题：如何自动发现代码大语言模型中的不一致程序行为？为了解决这一挑战，我们提出了一种自动一致性测试方法，称为MUCOCO，它采用语义保持的变异分析来暴露代码大语言模型中的不一致行为。给定一个编码查询，MUCOCO自动将其程序转换为语义等价的程序（即变异体），并检测变异体与原始程序之间的不一致性（例如，不同的输出或测试失败）。我们使用四个（4）编码任务和七个（7）大语言模型评估了MUCOCO。结果表明，MUCOCO在暴露不一致性方面是有效的，并且优于最接近的基线（TURBULENCE）。MUCOCO生成的输入中约有七分之一（15%）暴露了不一致性。我们的工作激励了测试代码大语言模型一致性属性的需求。

Original abstract: Code LLMs often portray inconsistent program behaviors. Developers typically employ benchmarks to assess Code LLMs, but most benchmarks are hand-crafted, static and do not target consistency property. In this work, we pose the scientific question: how can we automatically discover inconsistent program behaviors in Code LLMs? To address this challenge, we propose an automated consistency testing method, called MUCOCO, which employs semantic-preserving mutation analysis to expose inconsistent behaviors in code LLMs. Given a coding query, MUCOCO automatically transforms its program into semantically equivalent programs (aka mutants) and detects inconsistencies between the mutants and the original program (e.g., different output or test failure). We evaluate MUCOCO using four (4) coding tasks and seven (7) LLMs. Results show that MUCOCO is effective in exposing inconsistency and outperforms the closest baseline (TURBULENCE). About one in seven (15%) inputs generated by MUCOCO exposed inconsistencies. Our work motivates the need to test Code LLMs for consistency property

</details>


### [4] [Towards More Empathic Programming Environments: An Experimental Empathic AI-Enhanced IDE](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19142v1)
*Justin Rainier Go,Kurt Christian Andaya,Roemer Gabriel Caliboso,Aaron Daniel Go,Jocelynn Cu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究介绍了关怀共情C IDE（Ceci），并通过与VSCode+ChatGPT的对比实验发现，共情响应在错误纠正上更有帮助，但未能显著改善学习效果或降低工作负荷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI在软件开发中的普及可能导致新手程序员过度依赖，缺乏批判性思维，因此需要一种优先考虑学习和情感支持的编程环境。

Method: 研究人员进行了比较性试点研究，让参与者使用Ceci或VSCode+ChatGPT完成编程任务，然后通过NASA-TLX工作负荷评估和可用性调查进行评价。

Result: 实验组和对照组在感知有效性、学习和工作负荷上无显著差异，但Ceci用户在错误纠正的感知帮助性上显著更高（p=0.0220）。

Conclusion: 共情响应本身不足以提升学习效果，需要进一步研究更大样本、多样化任务和更好的用户界面整合。

中文摘要：随着生成式人工智能成为软件开发不可或缺的一部分，过度依赖和批判性思维减弱的风险日益增加。本研究介绍了“Ceci”，我们的关怀共情C IDE，旨在通过优先考虑学习和情感支持而非直接代码生成来支持新手程序员。研究人员在Ceci与VSCode + ChatGPT [9, 40]之间进行了一项比较性试点研究。参与者完成了一项编程任务，并使用NASA-TLX工作负荷评估和测试后可用性调查进行了评价。尽管样本量较小（n=11），结果显示实验组（Ceci）和对照组在感知有效性、学习和工作负荷方面没有显著差异，但Ceci用户在错误纠正的感知帮助性上显著更高（p=0.0220）。这些发现表明，共情响应本身可能不足以增强学习者的成果、感知或减少工作负荷。总体而言，本研究为未来研究提供了基础框架。此类研究应探索更大的样本量、多样化的编程任务以及额外的共情特征，以更好地理解共情编程环境在支持新手程序员方面的潜力；同时必须确保共情特征在用户界面中得到良好整合。

Original abstract: As generative AI becomes integral to software development, the risk of over-reliance and diminished critical thinking grows. This study introduces "Ceci," our Caring Empathic C IDE designed to support novice programmers by prioritizing learning and emotional support over direct code generation. The researchers conducted a comparative pilot study between Ceci and VSCode + ChatGPT [9, 40]. Participants completed a coding task and were evaluated using the NASA-TLX workload assessment and a post-test usability survey. Although the sample size was small (n = 11), results show that there is no significant difference in perceived effectiveness, learning and workload between the Experimental Ceci group and the Control group, though Ceci users reported significantly greater perceived helpfulness in error correction (p = 0.0220). These findings suggest that empathic responses may not be sufficient on their own to enhance the learner's outcomes, perceptions, or reduce workload. Overall, this study provides a foundational framework for future research. Such research should explore larger sample sizes, diverse programming tasks, and additional empathic features to better understand the potential of empathic programming environments in supporting novice programmers; they must also ensure that the empathic features are well-integrated in the user interface.

</details>


### [5] [Cascaded Code Editing: Large-Small Model Collaboration for Effective and Efficient Code Editing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19201v1)
*Chaozheng Wang,Zezhou Yang,Shuzheng Gao,Cuiyun Gao,Zongjie Li,Yichen Li,Ting Peng,Hailiang Huang,Yuetang Deng,Michael R. Lyu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过将代码编辑分解为编辑草图生成（大模型）和草图应用（小模型）的两阶段级联，提高了效率，但需提升小模型的长上下文和跨文件处理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在代码编辑中生成完整文件效率低下，小模型虽高效但缺乏长上下文理解能力，需兼顾效率与效果。

Method: 提出两阶段级联：大模型生成简洁的编辑草图（高难度），小模型将草图应用到原始代码（低难度），减少大模型生成token数。

Result: 提高了整体效率，但小模型在长上下文和跨文件依赖场景下的草图应用能力受限。

Conclusion: 需进一步增强小模型在长上下文和跨文件场景下的草图应用能力，以提升级联方法的有效性。

中文摘要：代码编辑构成了软件开发中的一项基本实践，开发者根据自然语言需求修改现有代码库。准确的代码编辑需要全面理解现有代码库和修改需求。尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在代码编辑任务中展现出有前景的性能，但它们通过生成主要由未更改代码组成的完整修改文件而遭受显著的低效率。虽然较小的模型可能解决这种低效率问题，但它们通常缺乏有效理解准确编辑所需的长代码上下文的能力。为了确保有效性和效率，我们提出将代码编辑分解为两阶段级联：**编辑草图生成**，其中大型模型首先生成代表所需修改的简洁草图（更具挑战性的阶段），以及**编辑草图应用**，其中较小的模型将这些草图集成到原始代码中，以生成最终输出的编辑代码（较简单的阶段）。这种级联设计减少了大型模型生成的令牌数量，因为大部分输出由更小、更高效的模型处理，从而提高了整体效率。然而，这种方法的有效性受到当前小模型在处理长上下文场景和跨文件依赖关系方面能力有限（这些对于真实代码库中准确的草图应用至关重要）的约束。为了解决这些限制并增强小模型的草图应用能力，...

Original abstract: Code editing constitutes a fundamental practice in software development, wherein developers modify existing codebases according to natural language requirements. Accurate code editing necessitates a comprehensive understanding of both the existing codebase and the modification requirements. Although large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated promising performance in code editing tasks, they suffer from substantial inefficiency by generating entire modified files that largely consist of unchanged code. While smaller models could potentially address this inefficiency, they typically lack the capacity to effectively comprehend long code contexts required for accurate editing. To ensure both effectiveness and efficiency, we propose to decompose code editing into a two-stage cascade: \textbf{edit sketch generation}, wherein a large model first produces concise sketches representing the requisite modifications (the more challenging phase), and \textbf{edit sketch application}, wherein a smaller model integrates these sketches into the original code to produce the final output edited code (the simpler phase). This cascaded design reduces the number of tokens generated by the large model, as the majority of the output is handled by the smaller, more efficient model, thereby enhancing overall efficiency. However, the effectiveness of this approach is constrained by current small models' limited capabilities in handling long-context scenarios and cross-file dependencies, which are essential for accurate sketch application in real-world codebases. To address these limitations and enhance smaller models' sketch application capabilities, ...

</details>


### [6] [iCoRe: An Iterative Correlation-Aware Retriever for Bug Reproduction Test Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19224v2)
*Junyi Wang,Jialun Cao,Zhongxin Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: iCoRe是一种迭代、相关性感知的上下文检索方法，通过差异化检索源代码与测试用例、融合语义与函数调用关系、以及建立检索与生成阶段的反馈循环，显著提升了LLM生成bug复现测试的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-based BRT方法依赖的检索策略存在三大局限：统一检索忽视源代码与测试用例的不同需求、仅用语义相似性忽略函数调用关系、缺乏生成阶段反馈导致无法优化上下文，共同造成低质量上下文，阻碍bug复现准确性。

Method: 提出iCoRe，显式建模三种关键相关性：1）源代码与测试用例的差异化检索；2）文本语义与函数调用结构的相关性评估；3）检索与生成阶段的迭代反馈与优化，从而实现高质量上下文检索。

Result: 在SWT-bench Lite和TDD-bench Verified上，iCoRe分别达到42.0%和52.8%的Fail-to-Pass率，相比现有检索方法相对提升19.7%-31.7%。

Conclusion: iCoRe通过相关性感知的迭代上下文检索有效克服了现有方法的局限，显著提高了LLM生成bug复现测试的准确性。

中文摘要：从问题描述自动生成错误重现测试（BRT）对软件维护至关重要。基于LLM的方法在此任务中显示出巨大潜力。其有效性高度依赖于从代码库中检索高质量上下文。现有方法的检索阶段依赖于传统方法如BM25或LLM驱动的策略。基于LLM的检索策略通常为LLM配备工具，让其自主探索存储库或从提供的列表中选择最相关的文件和代码片段作为上下文。然而，这些检索方法存在三个关键限制：1）它们通常对源代码和测试用例采用统一的检索策略，忽视了它们不同的检索需求。2）它们仅关注语义相似性而忽略函数调用关系，导致不相关的上下文。3）检索缺乏来自生成阶段的反馈循环，无法基于执行结果优化上下文。这些限制共同导致低质量上下文，从而妨碍错误重现的准确性。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了iCoRe，一种迭代的、相关性感知的上下文检索方法，明确意识到了三种关键相关性：1）源代码和测试用例之间的相关性，需要差异化检索；2）文本语义与函数调用结构之间的相关性，以实现准确的相关性评估；3）检索与生成阶段之间的相关性，实现迭代反馈与优化。为了评估iCoRe，我们将其与基于LLM的BRT生成器集成，并在SWT-bench Lite和TDD-bench Verified基准上进行了全面评估。实验结果表明，我们的方法分别达到了42.0%和52.8%的Fail-to-Pass率，相对于现有的检索方法实现了19.7%-31.7%的相对改进。

Original abstract: Automatically generating bug reproduction tests (BRT) from issue descriptions is crucial for software maintenance. LLM-based approaches have shown great potential for this task. Their effectiveness heavily relies on retrieving high-quality context from the codebase. The retrieval phase of existing approaches relies on either traditional methods like BM25 or LLM-driven strategies. LLM-based retrieval strategies typically equip an LLM with tools to autonomously explore the repository or select the most relevant files and code snippets from a provided list as context. However, these retrieval methods suffer from three key limitations: 1) They often employ a unified strategy for retrieving both source code and test cases, overlooking their distinct retrieval requirements. 2) They focus solely on semantic similarity while ignoring function call relationships, leading to irrelevant context. 3) The retrieval lacks a feedback loop from the generation phase, preventing it from refining the context based on execution results. These limitations collectively result in low-quality context, thereby hindering the accuracy of bug reproduction. To address these challenges, we propose iCoRe, an iterative, correlation-aware context retrieval approach explicitly aware of three key correlations: 1) between source code and test cases, which requires differentiated retrieval, 2) between textual semantics and function call structures for accurate relevance assessment, and 3) between the retrieval and generation phases, which enables iterative feedback and refinement. To evaluate iCoRe, we integrate it with an LLM-based BRT generator and conduct a comprehensive evaluation on the SWT-bench Lite and TDD-bench Verified benchmarks. Experimental results show that our method achieves a Fail-to-Pass rate of 42.0% and 52.8% respectively, representing 19.7%-31.7% relative improvements over existing retrieval methods.

</details>


### [7] [DebugRepair: Enhancing LLM-Based Automated Program Repair via Self-Directed Debugging](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19305v1)
*Linhao Wu,Yifei Pei,Zhen Yang,Kainan Li,Zhonghang Lu,Hao Tan,Xiran Lyu,Jia Li,Yizhou Chen,Pengyu Xue,Kunwu Zheng,Dan Hao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出DebugRepair框架，通过模拟调试收集中间运行时证据，增强LLM的自动程序修复能力，在多个基准上达到最先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反馈式APR方法仅依赖结果级别的失败症状（如堆栈跟踪），缺乏中间运行时证据，导致LLM推断错误原因并生成错误补丁。

Method: DebugRepair包含三个组件：测试语义净化（减少噪声）、模拟插桩（收集运行时轨迹，含规则回退）和调试驱动的对话式修复（利用先前尝试和新状态逐步优化补丁）。

Result: 在Defects4J上，GPT-3.5修复224个错误（优于SOTA 26.2%），DeepSeek-V3修复295个错误（超基线59个）；在五个额外LLM上修复性能提升51.3%。

Conclusion: DebugRepair通过引入中间运行时证据显著提升LLM的APR性能，所有组件均有效，达到最先进水平。

中文摘要：自动程序修复（APR）得益于大型语言模型（LLM）的代码理解和生成能力。现有的基于反馈的APR方法通过使用测试执行反馈迭代优化候选补丁，并已显示出有前景的结果。然而，大多数方法依赖于结果级别的失败症状，例如堆栈跟踪，这些症状展示了失败如何被观测到，但未能暴露对根因分析至关重要的中间运行时状态。因此，LLM通常在没有足够运行时证据的情况下推断错误原因，导致错误的补丁。为解决这一局限，我们提出了DebugRepair，一个面向基于LLM的APR的自我导向调试框架。DebugRepair通过模拟调试收集的中间运行时证据来增强补丁优化。它由三个组件组成：测试语义净化、模拟插桩和调试驱动的对话式修复。它们共同减少嘈杂的测试上下文，通过带有规则回退的目标调试语句收集运行时轨迹，并利用先前的尝试和新观测到的运行时状态逐步优化候选补丁。我们在三个跨Java和Python的基准上评估DebugRepair。实验表明，DebugRepair在15种方法中达到了最先进的性能。使用GPT-3.5，它在Defects4J上正确修复了224个错误，比先前最先进的基于LLM的方法高出26.2%。使用DeepSeek-V3，它正确修复了295个Defects4J错误，超过了第二好的基线59个错误。在另外五个骨干LLM上，DebugRepair相较于普通设置将修复性能提升了51.3%。消融研究进一步确认了所有组件的有效性。

Original abstract: Automated Program Repair (APR) has benefited from the code understanding and generation capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). Existing feedback-based APR methods iteratively refine candidate patches using test execution feedback and have shown promising results. However, most rely on outcome-level failure symptoms, such as stack traces, which show how failures are observed but fail to expose the intermediate runtime states critical for root-cause analysis. As a result, LLMs often infer bug causes without sufficient runtime evidence, leading to incorrect patches. To address this limitation, we propose DebugRepair, a self-directed debugging framework for LLM-based APR. DebugRepair enhances patch refinement with intermediate runtime evidence collected through simulated debugging. It consists of three components: test semantic purification, simulated instrumentation, and debugging-driven conversational repair. Together, they reduce noisy test context, collect runtime traces through targeted debugging statements with rule-based fallback, and progressively refine candidate patches using prior attempts and newly observed runtime states. We evaluate DebugRepair on three benchmarks across Java and Python. Experiments show that DebugRepair achieves state-of-the-art performance against 15 approaches. With GPT-3.5, it correctly fixes 224 bugs on Defects4J, outperforming prior SOTA LLM-based methods by 26.2%. With DeepSeek-V3, it correctly fixes 295 Defects4J bugs, surpassing the second-best baseline by 59 bugs. Across five additional backbone LLMs, DebugRepair improves repair performance by 51.3% over vanilla settings. Ablation studies further confirm the effectiveness of all components.

</details>


### [8] [Improving LLM-Driven Test Generation by Learning from Mocking Information](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19315v1)
*Jamie Lee,Flynn Teh,Hengcheng Zhu,Mengzhen Li,Mattia Fazzini,Valerio Terragni*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: MOCKMILL通过利用开发者编写的测试中的mock信息，结合LLM和迭代修复，生成更有效的单元测试，覆盖代码行和杀死变异体方面优于现有测试和基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在单元测试生成中展示潜力，但现有方法未充分利用开发者已定义的mock信息，我们探索是否可以利用这些信息进一步提升生成质量。

Method: 提出MOCKMILL，自动从开发者编写的测试中提取mock信息（stubbings和交互期望），结合LLM和迭代生成-修复过程，生成针对被mock替换组件的测试用例。

Result: 在6个Java项目的10个类上，使用4种LLM评估，MOCKMILL生成的测试在代码行覆盖率和变异杀死率上均超过现有项目测试和基线方法生成的测试。

Conclusion: 初步证据表明，利用mock信息是增强基于LLM的测试生成的一种互补且有效的方式。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）最近在自动单元测试生成方面展现出强大潜力。这促使我们研究是否可以利用现有测试套件中开发者定义的测试替身（通常称为mock）来改进LLM驱动的测试生成。为此，我们提出了MOCKMILL，一种基于LLM的技术和工具，通过利用从开发者编写的测试中自动提取的mock信息来生成测试用例。MOCKMILL针对现有测试中被测试替身替换的组件，并利用编码的桩和交互期望来指导测试生成，结合迭代生成-修复流程确保可执行的测试。我们使用四个LLM对六个Java项目中的10个开源类评估了MOCKMILL，并将生成的测试与现有项目测试和基线方法生成的测试进行了比较。结果表明，MOCKMILL的测试覆盖了现有测试和基线生成测试未覆盖的代码行并杀死了变异体。总体而言，我们的发现提供了初步证据，表明利用mock信息是增强基于LLM的测试生成的一种互补且有效的方式。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have recently shown strong potential for automated unit test generation. This has motivated us to investigate whether developer-defined test doubles (commonly referred to as mocks) available in existing test suites can be leveraged to improve LLM-driven test generation. To this end, we propose MOCKMILL, an LLM-based technique and tool that generates test cases by exploiting mocking information automatically extracted from developer-written tests. MOCKMILL targets components that are replaced by test doubles in existing tests and uses the encoded stubbings and interaction expectations to guide test generation, combined with an iterative generation-and-repair process to ensure executable tests. We evaluated MOCKMILL on 10 open-source classes from six Java projects using four LLMs, and compared the generated tests with existing project tests and tests produced by baseline approaches. The results show that MOCKMILL's tests cover lines of code and kill mutants that existing tests and baseline-generated tests miss. Overall, our findings provide preliminary evidence that leveraging mocking information is a complementary and effective way to enhance LLM-based test generation.

Original abstract: Green software engineering is emerging as a crucial response to information technology's rising energy impact, especially in continuous development. However, there remain challenges in devising automated methods for identifying energy regressions across commits and their associated code change patterns. In particular, little effort has been put into automatically detecting regressions at the commit level by identifying statistically significant changes in energy consumption. In this paper, we introduce EnergyTrackr, an approach designed to detect energy regressions across multiple commits that can then be used to identify code anti-patterns potentially contributing to the increase of software energy consumption over time. We describe our empirical evaluation, including repository mining and source code analysis, made on 3,232 commits from three Java projects, and show the approach's ability to identify significant energy changes. We also highlight recurring anti-patterns such as missing early exits or costly dependency upgrades. We expect EnergyTrackr to assist developers in accurately monitoring energy regressions and improvements within their projects, identifying code anti-patterns, and helping them optimize their source code to reduce software energy consumption.

### [10] [Towards Formalising Stakeholder Context using SysML v2](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19390v1)
*Matthew Harrison,John Carlin,Chengyuan Liu,Sarah Dunnett,Siyuan Ji*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一个结合SSM和SysML v2的框架，将主观利益相关者上下文映射到形式化系统架构，并通过案例验证可追溯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决主观利益相关者上下文与形式化系统架构之间的鸿沟，减少误解风险。

Method: 使用软系统方法论（SSM）和SysML v2，基于KerML和ISO 42010定义参考架构，实现从SSM输出到SysML v2概念的映射。

中文摘要：本文提出了一个框架，用于弥合主观利益相关者上下文与正式系统架构之间的差距。这是通过使用软系统方法论（SSM）和系统建模语言第2版（SysML v2）实现的。该方法利用内核建模语言（KerML）的精度以及SysML v2与ISO 42010的对齐，定义了一个参考架构，用于将SSM输出映射到SysML v2概念（例如利益相关者和关注点）。通过案例研究演示了该框架的应用，突出了从利益相关者上下文到系统架构的可追溯路径。与较不正式的方法相比，SysML v2的结构化映射和增加的语义精度预计将降低误解的风险，但跨不同利益相关者上下文的实证验证仍有待未来工作。主要识别出的权衡是与SysML v2的文本符号相关的入门门槛提高。

Original abstract: This paper presents a framework to bridge the gap between subjective stakeholder context and formal system architecture. This is achieved using Soft Systems Methodology (SSM) and Systems Modelling Language version 2 (SysML v2). The methodology utilises the precision of Kernel Modelling Language (KerML) and the alignment of SysML v2 with ISO 42010 to define a reference architecture for the mapping of SSM outputs to SysML v2 concepts such as stakeholders and concerns. Application of the framework is demonstrated through the use of a case study, highlighting the traceable path from stakeholder context to system architecture. The structured mapping and increased semantic precision of SysML v2 are anticipated to reduce the risk of misinterpretation compared to less formal approaches, though empirical validation across diverse stakeholder contexts remains as future work. The primary identified trade-off is the increased barrier to entry associated with SysML v2's textual notation.

### [11] [CASCADE: Detecting Inconsistencies between Code and Documentation with Automatic Test Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19400v1)
*Tobias Kiecker,Jan Arne Sparka,Martin Reuter,Albert Ziegler,Lars Grunske*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: CASCADE是一种利用大语言模型从文档生成单元测试，并交叉验证以低误报率检测代码-文档不一致的新型工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码与文档之间的不一致即使微小也会导致API用户混淆、引入新错误和增加维护成本，而自动检测中的误报会浪费开发者时间并阻碍实际采用。

Method: CASCADE利用大语言模型从自然语言文档生成单元测试，同时从文档生成代码进行交叉验证；仅当现有代码未通过测试而生成的代码通过时才报告不一致。

Result: 在71个不一致和814个一致的代码-文档对数据集上评估，并在Java、C#和Rust仓库中发现13个未知不一致，其中10个已被修复。

Conclusion: CASCADE展示了高精确性和对真实代码库的适用性，能有效发现并帮助修复代码-文档不一致。

中文摘要：在代码和文档之间保持一致是软件开发中一个至关重要但经常被忽视的方面。即使是微小的不匹配也可能混淆API用户，引入新错误，并增加整体维护工作量。这产生了对自动化解决方案的需求，以帮助开发者识别代码-文档不一致。然而，由于自动报告仍需要人工确认，误报会带来严重后果：浪费开发者时间并阻碍实际采用。我们介绍了CASCADE（通过执行进行源代码和文档的一致性分析），这是一种新型工具，用于检测不一致性，并特别强调减少误报。CASCADE利用大型语言模型（LLM）直接从自然语言文档生成单元测试。由于这些测试来源于文档，执行期间的任何失败都表明代码的文档行为和实际行为之间存在潜在不匹配。为了最小化误报，CASCADE还从文档生成代码以交叉检查生成的测试。根据设计，仅当满足两个条件时报告不一致：现有代码未能通过测试，而从文档生成的代码通过了相同的测试。我们在一个包含来自开源Java项目的71对不一致和814对一致的代码-文档对的新数据集上评估了CASCADE。此外，我们将CASCADE应用于其他Java、C#和Rust仓库，发现了13个先前未知的不一致性，其中10个随后已被修复，展示了CASCADE的精确性及其对真实代码库的适用性。

Original abstract: Maintaining consistency between code and documentation is a crucial yet frequently overlooked aspect of software development. Even minor mismatches can confuse API users, introduce new bugs, and increase overall maintenance effort. This creates demand for automated solutions that can assist developers in identifying code-documentation inconsistencies. However, since automatic reports still require human confirmation, false positives carry serious consequences: wasting developer time and discouraging practical adoption.
  We introduce CASCADE (Consistency Analysis for Source Code And Documentation through Execution), a novel tool for detecting inconsistencies with a strong emphasis on reducing false positives. CASCADE leverages Large Language Models (LLMs) to generate unit tests directly from natural-language documentation. Since these tests are derived from the documentation, any failure during execution indicates a potential mismatch between the documented and actual behavior of the code. To minimize false positives, CASCADE also generates code from the documentation to cross-check the generated tests. By design, an inconsistency is reported only when two conditions are met: the existing code fails a test, while the code generated from the documentation passes the same test.
  We evaluated CASCADE on a novel dataset of 71 inconsistent and 814 consistent code-documentation pairs drawn from open-source Java projects. Further, we applied CASCADE to additional Java, C#, and Rust repositories, where we uncovered 13 previously unknown inconsistencies, of which 10 have subsequently been fixed, demonstrating both CASCADE's precision and its applicability to real-world codebases.

</details>

*Wander Nauta,Marcus Gerhold,Marieke Huisman*

Method: 将模糊测试应用于演绎验证器，开发原型工具AValAnCHE并与VerCors验证器集成，通过生成随机输入来测试验证器的鲁棒性。

Original abstract: As deductive verifiers mature, their potential user base is growing from the initial core developers to other users. To convince external users of the suitability of verifiers, these tools must run reliably out of the box, give meaningful error messages and display correct results. Yet deductive verifiers are large and complex software systems and their own full verification is often out of reach. We therefore need complementary means to provide such guarantees. This paper advocates the use of fuzzing as a practical way to improve the quality and robustness of deductive verifiers. We outline how fuzz testing can be applied to deductive verifiers, and demonstrate the idea with the prototype tool AValAnCHE, which is integrated with the VerCors verifier. We report on our experiments in which AValAnCHE uncovered several issues in VerCors and demonstrate that the approach also works for other deductive verifiers

### [13] [On Reasoning-Centric LLM-based Automated Theorem Proving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19558v1)
*Yican Sun,Chengwei Shi,Hangzhou Lyu,Yingfei Xiong*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出ReCent-Prover，通过反思验证和基于规划的检索提升自动定理证明能力，在CoqStoq基准上提升22.58%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有证明代理未充分利用LLM在高层次规划和自我批判方面的推理能力。

Method: 提出验证与反思（validation with reflection）和基于规划的检索（retrieval with planning）两种技术。

Result: 在CoqStoq基准上，相同预算下定理证明数量相对提升22.58%。

Conclusion: 以推理为中心的设计显著增强了自动定理证明能力。

中文摘要：自动定理证明是形式化方法的基础，最近的趋势是将大型语言模型（LLM）与证明助手集成，形成有效的证明代理。虽然现有的证明代理表现出良好的性能，但它们并未充分利用现代LLM在高层次规划和自我批判方面的推理能力。我们认为，证明代理不仅应生成策略，还应战略性地推理证明计划，并批判性地评估自己的提议。本文介绍了ReCent-Prover，一种以推理为中心的基于LLM的Rocq证明代理，解决了当前系统的两个关键限制。首先，我们提出了带有反思的验证，使LLM能够审视其生成的策略，并在反思发现潜在错误时综合失败总结，从而更早地过滤掉可能误用的策略。其次，我们提出了带有规划的检索，该检索以LLM生成的证明计划为条件，而不是子目标相似性，检索与预期证明策略一致的引理和证明。这两种技术都增加了LLM的调用次数。然而，在CoqStoq基准测试上，即使在相同的LLM调用次数预算下，ReCent-Prover在证明定理的数量上比之前的最先进技术提高了22.58%，表明我们的以推理为中心的设计显著增强了自动定理证明能力。

Original abstract: Automated theorem proving is fundamental to formal methods, and the recent trend is to integrate large language models (LLMs) and proof assistants to form effective proof agents. While existing proof agents show promising performance, they inadequately leverage reasoning capabilities of modern LLMs in high-level planning and self-critique. We argue that proof agents should not merely generate tactics but also reason strategically about proof plans and critically evaluate their own proposals.
  This paper introduces ReCent-Prover, a reasoning-centric LLM-based proof agent for Rocq that addresses two critical limitations in current systems. First, we present validation with reflection, enabling LLMs to scrutinize their generated tactics and synthesize failure summaries when reflection identifies potential errors, filtering out potentially misapplied tactics earlier. Second, we propose retrieval with planning, which conditions retrieval on LLM-generated proof plans rather than subgoal similarity, retrieving lemmas and proofs that align with the anticipated proof strategy. Both techniques increase the number of invocations of LLMs. However, when evaluated on the CoqStoq benchmark, even under the same budget of LLM invocations, ReCent-Prover achieves a 22.58% relative improvement in the number of proved theorems over the previous state-of-the-art, demonstrating that our reasoning-centric design significantly enhances automated theorem proving capabilities.

</details>


### [14] [Predictive Autoscaling for Node.js on Kubernetes: Lower Latency, Right-Sized Capacity](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19705v2)
*Ivan Tymoshenko,Luca Maraschi,Matteo Collina*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于集群范围聚合的预测性扩展算法，消除反馈回路，在基准测试中相比HPA和KEDA显著降低延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kubernetes现有扩展机制（HPA和KEDA）是反应式的，检测到过载后才扩展，导致延迟SLO违规；即使降低阈值也会造成过度配置。

Method: 定义指标模型（三个函数）和五阶段流水线，使用集群范围聚合（在扩展下近似不变）作为稳定信号，通过短期外推预测未来负载并主动扩展。

Result: 在稳定斜坡和突然尖峰场景下，算法使实例负载保持目标阈值附近；稳定斜坡中位数延迟26ms，远低于KEDA的154ms和HPA的522ms。

Conclusion: 预测性扩展算法通过消除反馈回路和利用集群聚合信号，有效提升响应性和资源利用率，优于现有反应式方法。

中文摘要：Kubernetes提供了两种默认的扩展Node.js工作负载的路径，两者都有结构上的局限性。水平Pod自动扩缩器（HPA）基于CPU利用率进行扩展，但这并不直接测量事件循环饱和度：Node.js Pod可能会排队请求并错过延迟SLO，而CPU报告的使用率却是适中的。KEDA通过更丰富的触发器（包括事件循环指标）扩展了HPA，但继承了相同的反应式控制循环，只有在过载已经开始后才检测到。到新Pod启动并吸收流量时，系统可能已经降级。降低阈值改变了工作点，但没有改变动态：扩缩器仍然对已经超过的值做出反应，代价是永久性的过度配置。
我们提出了一种预测性扩展算法，该算法预测在容量准备好时负载将处于什么位置，并基于该预测主动进行扩展。每个实例的指标会被扩缩器自身的操作所污染：添加一个实例会重新分配负载并改变每个指标，即使外部流量没有变化。我们观察到，操作一个在扩展下近似不变的集群范围聚合消除了这个反馈回路，产生了一个适合短期外推的稳定信号。
我们定义了一个指标模型（一组三个函数，描述特定指标如何与扩展相关）和一个五阶段流水线，将原始的、不规则时间的、部分指标数据转换为干净的预测信号。在与HPA和KEDA的基准测试中，在稳定斜坡和突然尖峰两种场景下，该算法使每个实例的负载保持在目标阈值附近。在稳定斜坡下，中位数延迟为26ms，而KEDA为154ms，HPA为522ms。

Original abstract: Kubernetes offers two default paths for scaling Nodejs workloads, and both have structural limitations. The Horizontal Pod Autoscaler scales on CPU utilization, which does not directly measure event loop saturation: a Node.js pod can queue requests and miss latency SLOs while CPU reports moderate usage. KEDA extends HPA with richer triggers, including event-loop metrics, but inherits the same reactive control loop, detecting overload only after it has begun. By the time new pods start and absorb traffic, the system may already be degraded. Lowering thresholds shifts the operating point but does not change the dynamic: the scaler still reacts to a value it has already crossed, at the cost of permanent over-provisioning.
  We propose a predictive scaling algorithm that forecasts where load will be by the time new capacity is ready and scales proactively based on that forecast. Per-instance metrics are corrupted by the scaler's own actions: adding an instance redistributes load and changes every metric, even if external traffic is unchanged. We observe that operating on a cluster-wide aggregate that is approximately invariant under scaling eliminates this feedback loop, producing a stable signal suitable for short-term extrapolation.
  We define a metric model (a set of three functions that encode how a specific metric relates to scaling) and a five-stage pipeline that transforms raw, irregularly-timed, partial metric data into a clean prediction signal. In benchmarks against HPA and KEDA under steady ramp and sudden spike, the algorithm keeps per-instance load near the target threshold throughout. Under the steady ramp, median latency is 26ms, compared to 154ms for KEDA and 522ms for HPA.

</details>


### [15] [PlayCoder: Making LLM-Generated GUI Code Playable](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19742v1)
*Zhiyuan Peng,Wei Tao,Xin Yin,Chenhao Ying,Yuan Luo,Yiwen Guo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出PlayEval基准和PlayCoder框架，用于评估和改进LLM生成GUI应用（含游戏）的逻辑正确性，发现现有模型在Play@3上近乎为零，而PlayCoder显著提升至20.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码生成基准主要通过测试用例评估，不适用于交互式、事件驱动的GUI应用，需要关注交互流程和UI逻辑的正确性。

Method: 构建PlayEval基准（43个多语言GUI应用）和Play@k指标，开发PlayTester基于LLM的智能体进行自动化逻辑检测，提出PlayCoder多智能体闭环框架用于生成、评估和迭代修复。

Result: 10个代码LLM在Play@3上近乎为零，PlayCoder将Play@3提升至20.3%（Exec@3达38.1%），并能发现并修复静默逻辑错误。

Conclusion: PlayCoder有效提升GUI应用生成的功能正确性和语义对齐，弥补了传统指标的不足。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在代码生成方面取得了强劲成果，但它们生成GUI应用程序（尤其是游戏）的能力仍未得到充分研究。现有基准主要通过测试用例评估正确性，但这对于GUI应用程序是不充分的，因为这些系统是交互式的、事件驱动的，并且需要在用户操作序列中实现正确的状态转换。因此，评估应考虑交互流程和UI逻辑，而不仅仅是通过/失败的结果。为了研究这个问题，我们引入了PlayEval，一个基于仓库的基准，由43个多语言GUI应用程序（Python、TypeScript和JavaScript）构建。与难以适应桌面环境的先前GUI基准不同，PlayEval涵盖六种主要的GUI应用类别，并直接支持代码生成评估。我们进一步提出了Play@k，一种衡量在k个候选生成中至少有一个可以在没有逻辑错误的情况下端到端可玩性的指标。为了支持可靠的评估，我们开发了PlayTester，一个基于LLM的智能体，执行面向任务的GUI试玩并自动检测逻辑违规。在10个最先进的代码LLM上的实验表明，尽管编译率很高，但它们的Play@3几乎为零，揭示了生成逻辑正确的GUI应用程序方面的重大弱点。为了解决这一局限性，我们提出了PlayCoder，一个多智能体、基于仓库的框架，以闭环方式生成、评估和迭代修复GUI应用程序代码。PlayCoder显著提高了开源和闭源模型的功能正确性和语义对齐，达到了高达38.1%的Exec@3和20.3%的Play@3。案例研究进一步表明，它可以发现传统指标遗漏的静默逻辑错误，并通过有针对性的编辑进行修复。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have achieved strong results in code generation, but their ability to generate GUI applications, especially games, remains insufficiently studied. Existing benchmarks mainly evaluate correctness through test cases, which are inadequate for GUI applications because these systems are interactive, event-driven, and require correct state transitions across sequences of user actions. Their evaluation therefore should consider interaction flows and UI logic rather than only pass/fail outcomes. To study this problem, we introduce PlayEval, a repository-aware benchmark built from 43 multilingual GUI applications in Python, TypeScript, and JavaScript. Unlike prior GUI benchmarks that are difficult to adapt to desktop environments, PlayEval covers six major GUI application categories and directly supports code-generation evaluation. We further propose Play@k, a metric that measures whether at least one of *k* generated candidates can be played end-to-end without logical errors. To support reliable evaluation, we develop PlayTester, an LLM-based agent that performs task-oriented GUI playthroughs and detects logic violations automatically. Experiments on 10 state-of-the-art code LLMs show that, despite high compilation rates, they achieve near-zero Play@3, revealing major weaknesses in generating logically correct GUI applications. To address this limitation, we present PlayCoder, a multi-agent, repository-aware framework that generates, evaluates, and iteratively repairs GUI application code in a closed loop. PlayCoder substantially improves both functional correctness and semantic alignment for open-source and closed-source models, reaching up to 38.1% Exec@3 and 20.3% Play@3. Case studies further show that it can uncover silent logic bugs missed by traditional metrics and fix them through targeted edits.

### [16] [ViBR: Automated Bug Replay from Video-based Reports using Vision-Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19905v1)
*Sidong Feng,Dingbang Wang,Nikola Tomic,Tingting Yu,Aldeida Aleti,Chunyang Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ViBR是一种轻量级且全自动的方法，使用CLIP和视觉语言模型从GUI屏幕录制中重现错误，实现了72%的重现率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有从GUI录制中重现错误的方法依赖于脆弱的启发式方法或需要大量的工具支持，限制了其适用性。

Method: ViBR使用基于CLIP的嵌入相似性进行动作边界分割，并结合视觉语言模型进行区域感知的GUI状态比较和引导的错误回放。

Result: ViBR成功重现了72%的错误录制，显著优于最先进的基线和消融变体。

Conclusion: ViBR证明了结合CLIP和视觉语言模型能够从GUI录制中实现有效且全自动的错误重现，无需特定应用的设置。

中文摘要：错误报告在软件维护中起着关键作用，帮助用户向开发者传达遇到的问题。最近，GUI屏幕录制视频作为一种错误报告工件越来越受欢迎，因为它们易于使用且能保留丰富的上下文信息。然而，从这些录制中自动重现错误仍然是一个重大挑战。现有方法通常依赖于脆弱的图像处理启发式方法、明确的触摸指示器或预构建的UI转换图，这些都需要重要的工具支持和特定应用的设置。本文提出了ViBR，一种轻量级且全自动的方法，直接从GUI录制中重现错误。具体来说，ViBR结合了基于CLIP的嵌入相似性用于动作边界分割，以及视觉语言模型（VLM）用于区域感知的GUI状态比较和引导的错误回放。实验结果表明，ViBR成功重现了72%的错误录制，显著优于最先进的基线和消融变体。

Original abstract: Bug reports play a critical role in software maintenance by helping users convey encountered issues to developers. Recently, GUI screen capture videos have gained popularity as a bug reporting artifact due to their ease of use and ability to retain rich contextual information. However, automatically reproducing bugs from such recordings remains a significant challenge. Existing methods often rely on fragile image-processing heuristics, explicit touch indicators, or pre-constructed UI transition graphs, which require non-trivial instrumentation and app-specific setup. This paper presents ViBR, a lightweight and fully automated approach that reproduces bugs directly from GUI recordings. Specifically, ViBR combines CLIP-based embedding similarity for action boundary segmentation with Vision-Language Models (VLMs) for region-aware GUI state comparison and guided bug replay. Experimental results show that ViBR successfully reproduces 72% of bug recordings, significantly outperforming state-of-the-art baselines and ablation variants.

### [17] [Insights into Security-Related AI-Generated Pull Requests](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19965v1)
*Md Fazle Rabbi,Asif K. Turzo,Arifa I. Champa,Minhaz F. Zibran*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 分析了超过33,000个AI生成的PR，发现安全相关的PR存在重复弱点（如正则低效、注入、路径遍历），许多有缺陷的PR被合并，拒绝多因社会因素，提交信息质量影响有限，并扩展了拒绝分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI编码代理的普及，其安全性和信任问题日益突出，但缺乏对AI生成PR中安全问题的系统性分析。

Method: 收集并分析了超过33,000个AI生成的PR，筛选出675个安全相关PR，通过定量和定性方法研究安全弱点、审查结果、提交信息质量等。

Result: 安全AI PR引入重复弱点（正则低效、注入、路径遍历），许多有缺陷PR被合并，拒绝源于不活跃或测试缺失，提交信息质量影响小，并扩展了拒绝分类。

Conclusion: AI编码代理在安全软件工程中既有优势也有不足，需关注其引入的重复弱点和社会因素导致的审查漏洞。

中文摘要：近年来，人工智能编码代理在协助人类开发者完成各种软件工程任务方面做出了越来越多的贡献。然而，这种日益增长的AI辅助自主性引发了关于安全和信任的问题。在本文中，我们分析了超过33,000个AI生成的拉取请求（PR），并识别出675个由智能体AI提交的与安全相关的提交。然后，我们研究了这些与安全相关的PR，重点关注重复出现的安全弱点、审查结果和延迟、提交信息质量以及拒绝原因。结果表明，与安全相关的AI PR引入了一小组重复出现的弱点，如正则表达式低效、注入缺陷和路径遍历。许多有缺陷的贡献仍被合并，而拒绝通常源于社会或过程因素，如不活跃或缺少测试覆盖。AI PR的提交信息质量对接受或延迟的影响有限，这与先前研究中人类PR的情况形成对比。我们还通过添加AI生成安全贡献所特有的类别来扩展现有的拒绝分类。这些发现为自主编码系统在安全软件开发中的优缺点提供了新的见解。

Original abstract: Recent years have experienced growing contributions of AI coding agents that assist human developers in various software engineering tasks. However, this growing AI-assisted autonomy raises questions about security and trust. In this paper, we analyze more than 33,000 AI-generated pull requests (PRs) and identify 675 security-related submissions made by agentic AIs. Then we examine the security-related PRs with a focus on recurring security weaknesses, review outcomes and latency, commit message quality, and rejection reasons. The results show that security-related AI PRs introduce a small set of recurring weaknesses such as regex inefficiencies, injection flaws, and path traversal. Many flawed contributions are still merged, while rejections often arise from social or process factors such as inactivity or missing test coverage. The commit message quality of AI PRs has a limited effect on acceptance or latency, in contrast to human PRs reported in previous studies. We also extend existing rejection taxonomies by adding categories that are unique to AI-generated security contributions. These findings offer new insights into the strengths and shortcomings of autonomous coding systems in secure software development.

### [18] [Biomedical systems biology workflow orchestration and execution with PoSyMed](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20906v1)
*Simon Süwer,Zoe Chervontseva,Kester Bagemihl,Jan Baumbach,Olga Tsoy,Andreas Maier*

TL;DR: PoSyMed是一个开放模块化平台，通过后端架构、容器化执行、持久状态和对话界面集成生物信息学工具，并利用大语言模型作为受监督的语义助手，以提高可重复性和透明性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用后端中心架构，结合正式工具描述、基于容器的构建执行、持久工作流状态和对话式用户界面；集成大语言模型作为有限语义助手，在类型化、验证且人类监督的环境中辅助工具识别、步骤提议和参数化。

Result: 在代表性生物学软件场景中评估了工作流支持、交互设计和平台可扩展性，平台已公开可用。

中文摘要：科学软件的快速增长给生物信息学研究带来了实际障碍。尽管强大的统计和基于人工智能（AI）的方法现已广泛可用，但其有效使用常常受到碎片化分发、文档不一致、依赖关系复杂以及执行环境难以复现的阻碍。因此，即使是经验丰富的用户，重新使用已发表的工具以及将工作流适配到自己的数据仍然在技术上要求高且耗时。在这里，我们提出PoSyMed，一个用于生物信息学工具和工作流的可控集成、组合和执行的开放模块化平台。PoSyMed结合了后端中心的平台架构与正式工具描述、受控的基于容器的构建和执行过程、持久的工作流状态以及基于对话的用户界面。大型语言模型（LLM）不是作为自主决策者集成，而是作为人类-计算机接口，其具有受限的语义助手，帮助识别工具、提出工作流步骤，并在类型化、经过验证和人类监督的执行环境中支持参数化。PoSyMed旨在提高实际生物医学分析在一个平台内的可重复性、可追溯性和透明性。我们描述了系统架构，并评估了其在代表性生物软件场景中在工作流支持、交互设计和平台可扩展性方面的行为。PoSyMed可在https://apps.cosy.bio/posymed公开获取。

Original abstract: The rapid growth of scientific software has created practical barriers for bioinformatics research. Although powerful statistical, artificial intelligence (AI)-based methods are now widely available, their effective use is often hindered by fragmented distribution, inconsistent documentation, complex dependencies, and difficult-to-reproduce execution environments. As a result, reusing published tools and workflow adaptation to own date remains technically demanding and time-intensive, even for experienced users. Here, we present PoSyMed, an open and modular platform for the controlled integration, composition, and execution of bioinformatics tools and workflows. PoSyMed combines a backend-centered platform architecture with formal tool descriptions, controlled container-based build and execution processes, persistent workflow state, and a dialogue-based user interface. Large language models (LLM) are integrated not as autonomous decision-makers, but as human-computer interface with bounded semantic assistants that help identify tools, propose workflow steps, and support parameterization within a typed, validated, and human-supervised execution environment. PoSyMed is designed to improve reproducibility, traceability, and transparency in practical biomedical analysis within one platform. We describe the system architecture and evaluate its behavior across representative biological software scenarios with respect to workflow support, interaction design, and platform extensibility. PoSyMed is publicly available at https://apps.cosy.bio/posymed.

### [19] [Automated Quantum Software and AI Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19970v1)
*Nazanin Siavash,Armin Moin*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过系统文献综述，分析了量子软件工程和量子人工智能中的（半）自动化方法，识别了近期趋势和未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于具备量子计算知识和技能的开发者和AI专家数量有限，自动化在量子计算、混合量子经典应用中尤为关键，有助于提升生产力和效率。

Method: 采用系统文献综述方法，聚焦于量子和混合量子经典应用中软件工程和人工智能的自动化技术，并识别趋势与未来方向。

Result: 识别了自动化在量子软件工程和量子人工智能中的近期趋势和未来方向，包括帮助决定应用部署的量子硬件和平台。

Conclusion: 自动化方法能够显著促进量子及混合AI驱动软件系统的更广泛开发与部署，尤其对于领域专家而言可实现生产力跃升。

中文摘要：在本文中，我们对量子软件工程（QSE）和量子人工智能（QAI）的（半）自动化方法进行了系统文献综述。先前文献中的研究表明，软件工程（SE）和人工智能（AI）实践可能通过使用（半）自动化方法变得更高效。这在量子计算（QC）、量子信息科学（QIS）和量子工程（QE）领域以及混合量子经典应用中同样适用。事实上，在这种情况下自动化甚至更为关键，因为具备所需量子计算知识和技能的开发者和AI专家（如数据科学家）数量有限。此外，在混合设置中，自动化有助于决定应用的哪一部分应部署在量子硬件上以及（如果适用）应在哪个可用的量子平台上部署。即使对于领域专家来说，这也有助于实现生产力跃升和效率提升。与先前的文献综述和调查不同，本研究聚焦于量子和混合量子经典应用的SE和AI中的自动化，并通过系统文献综述识别了近期趋势和未来方向。我们关注能够实现更广泛开发和部署量子及混合AI驱动软件系统的方法和技术。

Original abstract: In this paper, we conduct a systematic literature review of (semi-) automated approaches to Quantum Software Engineering (QSE) and Quantum Artificial Intelligence (QAI). Prior work in the literature indicated that both Software Engineering (SE) and Artificial Intelligence (AI) practices may become more efficient by using (semi-) automated approaches. This also holds in the Quantum Computing (QC), Quantum Information Science (QIS), and Quantum Engineering (QE) world, as well as in hybrid quantum-classical applications. In fact, automation is even more crucial in such cases since there is a limited number of developers and AI experts (e.g., data scientists) who possess the required knowledge and skills in QC. Moreover, in hybrid setups, automation may help decide what part of the application should be deployed on quantum hardware and on which of the available quantum platforms, if applicable. This can be a significant help to achieve productivity leap and efficiency even for subject matter experts. Unlike prior literature reviews and surveys, this work focuses on automation in SE and AI for quantum and hybrid quantum-classical applications and identifies the recent trends and future directions through a systematic literature review. We are interested in methods and techniques that can enable a broader development and deployment of quantum and hybrid AI-enabled software systems.

</details>


### [20] [FIKA: Expanding Dependency Reachability with Executability Guarantees](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20015v1)
*Yogya Gamage,Meriem Ben Chaaben,Martin Monperrus,Benoit Baudry*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出FIKA流水线，通过动态执行提供第三方库调用点的可执行性保证，在八个Java项目中将测试覆盖从54%提升至约74%，并改善了静态漏洞分析的优先级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有依赖可达性分析工具多为静态方法，缺乏执行信息，导致精度不足；需要一种动态方法来提供更强的可执行性保证。

Method: 提出FIKA流水线，自动生成可执行代码并执行，通过执行轨迹证明第三方库调用点的实际可达性。

Result: 在八个Java项目中，对2363个依赖方法验证了可执行性；将测试覆盖从54%提升20%（至约74%）；在六个项目中使超过75%的调用点可执行；改进了Semgrep的漏洞可达性分析结果。

Conclusion: FIKA通过动态执行有效提升了第三方库调用点的可执行性证明覆盖率，并能为静态可达性分析提供补充，帮助优先处理关键漏洞更新。

中文摘要：自动化第三方库分析工具通过解决关键的依赖管理挑战来帮助开发者，例如自动化版本更新、检测漏洞和检测破坏性更新。依赖可达性分析旨在通过将依赖问题空间缩小到真正重要的问题，来提高依赖管理的精度。大多数依赖可达性分析工具是静态的，并且根本上受限于缺乏执行。在本文中，我们提出了FIKA，一个为第三方库调用点提供可执行性保证的流水线。FIKA生成可执行的代码，其执行轨迹提供第三方库调用点实际可达的保证。我们将该方法应用于八个Java项目的数据集，以实证评估FIKA的有效性。平均而言，54%的调用点被现有测试套件覆盖，因此有证据表明它们可执行。FIKA进一步将这一覆盖率提高了20%，并能够演示2363个依赖方法的可执行性。在八个项目中的六个中，FIKA提供了强有力的保证，即超过75%的调用点可执行。我们进一步证明了FIKA能够改进Semgrep（一种最先进的静态漏洞可达性分析工具）提供的结果。我们表明，在Semgrep产生不确定的可达性结果的情况下，FIKA可以帮助优先处理具有更强可执行性保证的漏洞更新。

Original abstract: Automated third-party library analysis tools help developers by addressing key dependency management challenges, such as automating version updates, detecting vulnerabilities, and detecting breaking updates. Dependency reachability analysis aims at improving the precision of dependency management, by reducing the space of dependency issues to the ones that actually matter. Most tools for dependency reachability analysis are static and fundamentally limited by the absence of execution. In this paper, we propose FIKA, a pipeline for providing guarantees of executability for third-party library call sites. FIKA generates code that is executed, and whose execution trace provides guarantees that a third-party library call site is actually reachable. We apply our approach to a dataset of eight Java projects to empirically evaluate the effectiveness of FIKA. On average, 54% of these call sites are covered by the existing test suites, and therefore, have evidence for their executability. FIKA further improves this coverage by 20% and is able to demonstrate executability for 2363 dependency methods. In six out of eight projects, FIKA provides strong guarantees that more than 75% of call sites are executable. We further demonstrate that FIKA is capable of improving the results provided by Semgrep, a state-of-the-art static vulnerability reachability analysis tool. We show that FIKA can help prioritize the vulnerability updates with stronger guarantees of executability in cases where Semgrep yields inconclusive reachability results.

</details>

### [21] [AutomationBench](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18934v1)
*Daniel Shepard,Robin Salimans*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 跨应用工作流自动化基准，可迁移至coding agent评测

TL;DR: AutomationBench是一个评估AI智能体跨应用工作流编排能力的基准测试，任务覆盖多个领域，要求智能体自行发现API端点并遵循策略，当前最佳模型得分低于10%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试缺乏跨应用协调、API发现和策略遵循的结合，而实际业务工作流需要这些能力。

Method: 基于Zapier的实际工作流模式，构建涵盖销售、市场、运营等领域的任务，要求智能体自行发现API端点、遵循分层业务规则，在包含干扰记录的环境中执行，并通过最终状态评分。

Result: 即使最佳前沿模型得分也低于10%。

Conclusion: AutomationBench提供了一个具有挑战性的、现实的评估标准，揭示了当前模型与企业所需智能体能力之间的差距。

中文摘要：现有用于软件自动化的AI基准测试很少结合跨应用协调、自动API发现和策略遵循。实际业务工作流需要这三者：单个任务可能涉及CRM、邮箱、日历和即时通讯平台——要求智能体找到正确的端点、遵循策略文档并将正确数据写入每个系统。为解决这一差距，我们引入AutomationBench，一个通过REST API评估AI智能体跨应用工作流编排的基准测试。基于Zapier平台的实际工作流模式，任务涵盖销售、市场营销、运营、支持、财务和人力资源领域。智能体必须自行发现相关端点，遵循分层业务规则，并在包含无关甚至误导性记录的环境中导航。评分是程序化的且仅关注最终状态：正确数据是否最终落入正确的系统。即使最好的前沿模型目前得分也低于10%。AutomationBench提供了一个具有挑战性的、现实的衡量标准，表明当前模型相对于企业实际需要的智能体能力的位置。

Original abstract: Existing AI benchmarks for software automation rarely combine cross-application coordination, autonomous API discovery, and policy adherence. Real business workflows demand all three: a single task may span a CRM, inbox, calendar, and messaging platform - requiring the agent to find the right endpoints, follow a policy document, and write correct data to each system. To address this gap, we introduce AutomationBench, a benchmark for evaluating AI agents on cross-application workflow orchestration via REST APIs. Drawing on real workflow patterns from Zapier's platform, tasks span Sales, Marketing, Operations, Support, Finance, and HR domains. Agents must discover relevant endpoints themselves, follow layered business rules, and navigate environments with irrelevant and sometimes misleading records. Grading is programmatic and end-state only: whether the correct data ended up in the right systems. Even the best frontier models currently score below 10%. AutomationBench provides a challenging, realistic measure of where current models stand relative to the agentic capabilities businesses actually need.

</details>


### [22] [SAVOIR: Learning Social Savoir-Faire via Shapley-based Reward Attribution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18982v1)
*Xiachong Feng,Yi Jiang,Xiaocheng Feng,Deyi Yin,Libo Qin,Yangfan Ye,Lei Huang,Weitao Ma,Yuxuan Gu,Chonghan Qin,Bing Qin,Lingpeng Kong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于Shapley值的社交智能agent信用分配，可推广至coding agent训练

TL;DR: 提出SAVOIR框架，基于Shapley值公平分配信用，在社交强化学习中实现SOTA性能，7B模型超越大模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法对对话中信用分配的处理是回顾性的且缺乏理论基础，需要一种更合理的前瞻性公平分配机制。

Method: 采用期望效用将评估转为前瞻性估值，结合Shapley值确保公平的信用分配，并基于合作博弈论构建框架。

Result: 在SOTOPIA基准上所有设置达到新SOTA，7B模型匹配或超越GPT-4o和Claude-3.5-Sonnet，大型推理模型表现不佳。

Conclusion: 社交智能需要不同于分析推理的能力，现有推理模型在该任务上存在根本局限。

中文摘要：社交智能，即驾驭复杂人际互动的能力，是语言代理面临的一项基本挑战。通过强化学习训练此类代理需要解决信用分配问题：确定单个话语如何影响多轮对话结果。现有方法直接使用语言模型来分配回合级奖励，产生的归因是回顾性的且缺乏理论基础。我们提出了SAVOIR（社交强化学习的Shapley值），一个基于合作博弈论的新型原则性框架。我们的方法结合了两个互补原则：期望效用将评估从回顾性归因转变为前瞻性估值，捕获话语在实现有利未来轨迹方面的战略潜力；Shapley值确保公平的信用分配，具有效率性、对称性和边际性的公理保证。在SOTOPIA基准上的实验表明，SAVOIR在所有评估设置中实现了新的最先进性能，我们的7B模型匹配或超过了包括GPT-4o和Claude-3.5-Sonnet在内的专有模型。值得注意的是，即使是大型推理模型也持续表现不佳，这表明社交智能需要与分析推理性质不同的能力。

Original abstract: Social intelligence, the ability to navigate complex interpersonal interactions, presents a fundamental challenge for language agents. Training such agents via reinforcement learning requires solving the credit assignment problem: determining how individual utterances contribute to multi-turn dialogue outcomes. Existing approaches directly employ language models to distribute episode-level rewards, yielding attributions that are retrospective and lack theoretical grounding. We propose SAVOIR (ShApley Value fOr SocIal RL), a novel principled framework grounded in cooperative game theory. Our approach combines two complementary principles: expected utility shifts evaluation from retrospective attribution to prospective valuation, capturing an utterance's strategic potential for enabling favorable future trajectories; Shapley values ensure fair credit distribution with axiomatic guarantees of efficiency, symmetry, and marginality. Experiments on the SOTOPIA benchmark demonstrate that SAVOIR achieves new state-of-the-art performance across all evaluation settings, with our 7B model matching or exceeding proprietary models including GPT-4o and Claude-3.5-Sonnet. Notably, even large reasoning models consistently underperform, suggesting social intelligence requires qualitatively different capabilities than analytical reasoning.

</details>


### [23] [On Accelerating Grounded Code Development for Research](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19022v1)
*Santosh Ganji*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 面向科研coding agent的即时知识注入框架，直接相关coding agent

TL;DR: 该框架通过即时访问研究仓库和技术文档，解决了编码代理在专业领域缺乏最新知识的问题，加速了其集成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 专业科学技术领域缺乏对最新领域特定知识的访问，导致编码代理应用受限。

Method: 提出了一个开源框架，包括doc-search.dev文档上传和zed-fork领域规则执行。

Result: 实现了编码代理的实时上下文感知操作，加速了集成。

Conclusion: 该框架有效弥补了领域知识缺口，促进了编码代理在专业领域的应用。

中文摘要：专业科学技术领域在利用编码代理时面临的一个主要挑战是缺乏对最新领域特定知识的访问。基础模型通常在专业领域的推理能力有限，并且无法内化通过持续研究和实验不断发展的知识。探索新化合物的材料科学家、设计和评估新协议的通信工程师以及进行迭代实验的生物工程研究人员都面临这一限制。这些专家通常缺乏资源来微调大型模型或持续嵌入新发现，这给采用AI驱动的编码代理带来了障碍。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了一个框架，该框架使编码代理能够即时访问研究仓库和技术文档，从而实现实时的上下文感知操作。我们的开源实现允许用户通过doc-search.dev上传文档，并包含zed-fork，后者强制执行领域特定的规则和工作流。这些工具共同加速了编码代理在专业科学技术工作流中的集成。

Original abstract: A major challenge for niche scientific and technical domains in leveraging coding agents is the lack of access to up-to-date, domain- specific knowledge. Foundational models often demonstrate limited reasoning capabilities in specialized fields and cannot inherently incorporate knowledge that evolves through ongoing research and experimentation. Materials scientists exploring novel compounds, communication engineers designing and evaluating new protocols, and bioengineering researchers conducting iterative experiments all face this limitation. These experts typically lack the resources to fine-tune large models or continuously embed new findings, creating a barrier to adopting AI-driven coding agents. To address this, we introduce a framework that gives coding agents instanta- neous access to research repositories and technical documentation, enabling real-time, context-aware operation. Our open-source im- plementation allows users to upload documents via doc-search.dev and includes zed-fork, which enforces domain-specific rules and workflows. Together, these tools accelerate the integration of coding agents into specialized scientific and technical workflows

</details>


### [24] [OLLM: Options-based Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19087v1)
*Shashank Sharma,Janina Hoffmann,Vinay Namboodiri*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出选项化LLM，用潜在空间策略控制生成，对agent推理和控制有启发。

TL;DR: OLLM通过引入离散潜变量索引的选项集替代单一下一个词元预测，在1.7B模型上相较于LoRA基线在数学推理正确率上从51%提升至约70%，同时通过潜空间策略学习提升了可控性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准LLM依赖温度或采样启发式来诱导多样性，缺乏对多个合理下一个词元的显式建模，导致在数学推理等任务中可控性差、容易产生失调（如语言切换或退化推理）。

Method: OLLM在输出头前插入编码器和解码器，将单一下一个词元预测替换为由离散潜变量索引的选项集；然后在小潜空间中训练一个紧凑策略，通过选择潜变量控制生成。

Result: 在1.7B骨干模型上（仅1.56%参数可训练），OLLM在OmniMath上最优潜选择达到约70%正确率，远超LoRA基线的51%；潜空间策略学习使奖励优化更样本高效，并显著减少了常见失调。

Conclusion: 选项化的下一个词元建模增强了数学推理中的可控性、鲁棒性和效率，潜空间策略学习为LLM中强化学习提供了有前景的方向。

中文摘要：我们提出了选项LLM（OLLM），这是一种简单、通用的方法，将标准LLM的单个下一个词元预测替换为一组学习到的下一个词元选项，这些选项由离散潜变量索引。OLLM不依赖温度或采样启发式来诱导多样性，而是显式地建模变化：一个小的潜空间参数化多个合理的下一个词元选项，这些选项可以由下游策略选择或搜索。在架构上，OLLM是一个轻量级的“插件”，在输出层之前插入两层：一个编码器和一个解码器，从而允许几乎任何预训练LLM以最小的额外参数进行转换。我们将OLLM应用于一个1.7B参数的主干（仅1.56%的参数可训练），在OpenMathReasoning上训练，并在OmniMath上评估。最先进的LoRA适应基线在最终答案正确性上达到51%，而OLLM的选项集在最优潜变量选择下允许高达约70%。然后我们在潜空间中训练一个紧凑的策略，该策略发射潜变量以控制生成。在低维选项空间中操作使得奖励优化更加样本高效，并显著减少了常见的失调（例如，语言切换或退化推理），因为策略被约束在SFT期间学习到的选项上。关键的是，这种对齐源于模型结构，而不是额外的KL或手工设计的对齐损失。我们的结果表明，选项化的下一个词元建模增强了数学推理中的可控性、鲁棒性和效率，并突出了潜空间策略学习作为LLM中强化学习的一个有前景的方向。

Original abstract: We introduce Options LLM (OLLM), a simple, general method that replaces the single next-token prediction of standard LLMs with a \textit{set of learned options} for the next token, indexed by a discrete latent variable. Instead of relying on temperature or sampling heuristics to induce diversity, OLLM models variation explicitly: a small latent space parametrizes multiple plausible next-token options which can be selected or searched by a downstream policy. Architecturally, OLLM is a lightweight "plug-in" that inserts two layers: an encoder and a decoder, before the output head, allowing almost any pretrained LLM to be converted with minimal additional parameters. We apply OLLM to a 1.7B-parameter backbone (only $1.56\%$ of parameters trainable) trained on OpenMathReasoning and evaluated on OmniMath. The SOTA LoRA-adapted baselines peak at $51\%$ final answer correctness, while OLLM's option set allows up to $\sim 70\%$ under optimal latent selection. We then train a compact policy in the latent space that emits latents to control generation. Operating in a low-dimensional option space makes reward optimization far more sample-efficient and substantially reduces common misalignments (e.g., language switching or degenerate reasoning), as the policy is constrained to options learned during SFT. Crucially, this alignment arises from model structure rather than additional KL or handcrafted alignment losses. Our results demonstrate that optionized next-token modeling enhances controllability, robustness, and efficiency in math reasoning, and highlight latent-space policy learning as a promising direction for reinforcement learning in LLMs.

</details>


### [25] [How Much Thinking is Enough? Quantifying and Understanding Redundancy in LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23926v1)
*Zhiyuan Zhai,Xinkai You,Wenjing Yan,Xin Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 量化LLM推理冗余，对agent思考长度控制与效率优化有启发

TL;DR: 推理大模型的思维链存在大量冗余（61%-93%），且这种冗余是长度无关结果奖励的结构性后果，而非模型缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量和解释推理大模型长思维链中思考的必要性，揭示其冗余程度及根本原因。

Method: 形式化冗余度定义为正确轨迹中可截断而不影响答案的尾部比例；在四个模型和两个基准上大规模量化；并通过理论证明冗余是训练目标（长度无关结果奖励）的结构性结果。

Result: 步骤级冗余度一致很高（61%-93%），多数条件下中位数关键前缀仅为一个步骤；难度增加时冗余度下降但仍显著（46%-85%）；冗余度是长度无关结果奖励的必然结果，非模型特定。

Conclusion: 过度思考是当前推理模型训练方式（使用长度无关结果奖励）的结构性属性，而非可修补的bug。

中文摘要：具备推理能力的大语言模型通过生成长思维链来解决难题，但这会带来严重的延迟、GPU时间和能源消耗。粗略检查它们的轨迹可以发现大量的重新表述、验证和循环自我反思，然而这些思考中有多少实际上是必要的，从未在大规模上进行过衡量，也没有从第一性原理进行过解释。本文填补了这两个空白。
我们直接根据推理模型本身来形式化推理冗余度：正确轨迹的冗余度是其尾部可被截断的最大分段步骤比例，同时让模型π被迫终止思考并输出最终答案，仍能产生正确答案。在四个前沿推理模型和两个数学基准上进行的大规模量化表明，步骤级冗余度一致很高——在我们研究的8个（模型，基准）条件中，冗余度介于61%和93%之间，其中在八个条件中的六个，中位数关键前缀等于单个分段步骤——并且这一发现对评判器系列的选择具有鲁棒性，尽管在MATH-500上ρ随问题难度增加而下降，但即使在最难的Level-5问题上，所有四个模型仍然具有显著冗余（ρ ∈ [46%, 85%]）。
然后我们证明这种冗余度是长度无关结果奖励的结构性后果，而非模型特定伪影：在任何此类奖励下，不存在有限期望停止时间是最优的。该结果不依赖于强化学习算法、基础模型、数据分布，或策略是通过强化学习还是蒸馏获得的；因此，过度思考不是需要在单个模型中修补的bug，而是当前推理模型训练方式的结构性属性。代码：https://github.com/zhiyuanZhai20/how-much-thinking-is-enough

Original abstract: Reasoning-capable large language models solve hard problems by emitting long chains of thought, paying heavily in latency, GPU time, and energy. Casual inspection of their traces reveals extensive reformulation, verification, and circular self-reflection, yet how much of this deliberation is actually necessary has never been measured at scale or explained from first principles. This paper closes both gaps.
  We formalise reasoning redundancy directly in terms of the reasoning model itself: the redundancy of a correct trace is the largest fraction of its trailing segmented steps that can be truncated while $π$, forced to terminate thinking and emit a final answer, still produces the correct answer. A large-scale quantification across four frontier reasoning models and two mathematical benchmarks shows that step-level redundancy is consistently high -- between 61% and 93% across the 8 (model, benchmark) conditions we study, with the median critical prefix equal to a single segmented step in six of the eight conditions -- that the finding is robust to the choice of judge family, and that although $ρ$ decreases with problem difficulty on MATH-500, all four models remain substantially redundant ($ρ\in [46\%, 85\%]$) even on the hardest Level-5 problems.
  We then prove that this redundancy is a structural consequence of length-agnostic outcome rewards, not a model-specific artefact: under any such reward, no finite expected stopping time is optimal. The result holds regardless of RL algorithm, base model, data distribution, or whether the policy is obtained via RL or distillation; over-thinking is therefore not a bug to be patched in individual models but a structural property of how current reasoning models are trained. Code: https://github.com/zhiyuanZhai20/how-much-thinking-is-enough

</details>


### [26] [Forage V2: Knowledge Evolution and Transfer in Autonomous Agent Organizations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19837v1)
*Huaqing Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自主agent组织的知识积累与迁移架构，对多agent协作与长程任务有直接可迁移贡献

TL;DR: V2提出学习型组织架构，通过知识积累和跨模型迁移解决开放世界任务中的分母盲视问题，使弱智能体性能显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主智能体在开放世界任务中因缺乏明确完成边界而系统性地低估目标空间范围（分母盲视），需要有效的评估方法和知识积累机制。

Method: V2架构包括协同进化评估、方法隔离、组织记忆、审计分离和契约协议等制度设计，支持跨运行知识积累和跨模型知识迁移。

Result: 在网页抓取、API查询、数学推理三种任务上，知识条目从0增至54；弱智能体注入强智能体知识后覆盖差距从6.6pp降至1.1pp，成本减半，收敛轮数减半，且三次独立运行得到相同分母估计值266。

Conclusion: V2的贡献在于设计制度使任何智能体更可靠，积累的组织性、模型无关、可迁移知识以可读文档形式存储，可被未来任意智能体继承。

中文摘要：自主智能体在开放世界任务（其完成边界未事先给出）中运行时面临分母盲视：它们系统性地低估了目标空间的覆盖范围。Forage V1通过协同进化评估（独立的评估器发现“完整”的含义）和方法隔离（评估器和规划器无法看到彼此的代码）来解决这一问题。V2将架构从单次探索扩展为学习型组织：经验在多次运行中积累，跨模型能力迁移，并通过制度保障防止知识退化。我们通过三种任务类型（网页抓取、API查询、数学推理）展示了两个论断。知识积累：经过六次运行，知识条目从0增长到54，分母估计随着领域理解的加深而稳定。知识迁移：一个较弱的智能体（Sonnet）注入较强智能体（Opus）的知识后，将6.6个百分点的覆盖差距缩小到1.1个百分点，成本减半（从9.40美元降至5.13美元），收敛轮数减半（平均4.5轮 vs. 7.0轮），并且三次独立的注入运行得出完全相同的分母估计值（266），这表明组织知识本身校准了评估。V2的贡献在于架构：它设计了制度——审计分离、契约协议、组织记忆——使得任何智能体在进入时都更加可靠。积累的经验是组织性的、模型无关的、可迁移的，存储为可读文档，任何未来的智能体无论供应商或能力水平如何都可以继承。

Original abstract: Autonomous agents operating in open-world tasks -- where the completion boundary is not given in advance -- face denominator blindness: they systematically underestimate the scope of the target space. Forage V1 addressed this through co-evolving evaluation (an independent Evaluator discovers what "complete" means) and method isolation (Evaluator and Planner cannot see each other's code). V2 extends the architecture from a single expedition to a learning organization: experience accumulates across runs, transfers across model capabilities, and institutional safeguards prevent knowledge degradation.
  We demonstrate two claims across three task types (web scraping, API queries, mathematical reasoning). Knowledge accumulation: over six runs, knowledge entries grow from 0 to 54, and denominator estimates stabilize as domain understanding deepens. Knowledge transfer: a weaker agent (Sonnet) seeded with a stronger agent's (Opus) knowledge narrows a 6.6pp coverage gap to 1.1pp, halves cost (9.40 to 5.13 USD), converges in half the rounds (mean 4.5 vs. 7.0), and three independent seeded runs arrive at exactly the same denominator estimate (266), suggesting organizational knowledge calibrates evaluation itself.
  V2's contribution is architectural: it designs institutions -- audit separation, contract protocols, organizational memory -- that make any agent more reliable upon entry. The accumulated experience is organizational, model-agnostic, and transferable, stored as readable documents that any future agent inherits regardless of provider or capability level.

### [27] [ClawNet: Human-Symbiotic Agent Network for Cross-User Autonomous Cooperation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19211v1)
*Zhiqin Yang,Zhenyuan Zhang,Xianzhang Jia,Jun Song,Wei Xue,Yonggang Zhang,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多用户agent协作框架与身份治理机制，可迁移至coding agent协作场景。

TL;DR: 提出一种人类共生智能体范式，通过身份治理原语实现跨用户安全协作，并实例化为ClawNet框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI智能体系统仅服务单用户，缺乏跨用户协作的基础设施和治理机制，而人类生产力依赖于协作关系。

Method: 提出人类共生智能体范式，包含分层身份架构、范围授权和操作级责任性三个治理原语，并构建ClawNet框架。

Result: 在ClawNet中实现身份绑定和授权验证的中心协调器，支持多用户通过各自智能体安全协作。

Conclusion: AI智能体的下一个前沿在于数字化人类协作关系，而非提升个体能力。

中文摘要：当前的AI智能体框架在自动化单个任务方面取得了显著进展，然而所有现有系统都只为单个用户服务。人类生产力依赖于人们协调、协商和委派的社会和组织关系。当智能体从为一个人执行任务扩展到代表该人与他人协作时，支持跨用户智能体协作的基础设施完全缺失，更不用说确保其安全的治理机制了。我们认为，AI智能体的下一个前沿不在于更强的个体能力，而在于人类协作关系的数字化。为此，我们提出了一种人类共生智能体范式。每个用户拥有一个永久绑定的智能体系统，代表所有者进行协作，形成一个以人类为节点而非智能体的网络。该范式基于三个治理原语。分层身份架构将经理智能体与多个特定于上下文的身份智能体分离；经理智能体拥有全局知识，但在架构上隔离于外部通信。范围授权强制执行每个身份访问控制，并将边界违规升级给所有者。操作级责任性将每个操作记录在所有者身份和授权下，确保完全可审计。我们在ClawNet中实例化该范式，这是一个身份治理的智能体协作框架，通过中心协调器强制身份绑定和授权验证，使多个用户能够通过各自的智能体安全协作。

Original abstract: Current AI agent frameworks have made remarkable progress in automating individual tasks, yet all existing systems serve a single user. Human productivity rests on the social and organizational relationships through which people coordinate, negotiate, and delegate. When agents move beyond performing tasks for one person to representing that person in collaboration with others, the infrastructure for cross-user agent collaboration is entirely absent, let alone the governance mechanisms needed to secure it. We argue that the next frontier for AI agents lies not in stronger individual capability, but in the digitization of human collaborative relationships. To this end, we propose a human-symbiotic agent paradigm. Each user owns a permanently bound agent system that collaborates on the owner's behalf, forming a network whose nodes are humans rather than agents. This paradigm rests on three governance primitives. A layered identity architecture separates a Manager Agent from multiple context-specific Identity Agents; the Manager Agent holds global knowledge but is architecturally isolated from external communication. Scoped authorization enforces per-identity access control and escalates boundary violations to the owner. Action-level accountability logs every operation against its owner's identity and authorization, ensuring full auditability. We instantiate this paradigm in ClawNet, an identity-governed agent collaboration framework that enforces identity binding and authorization verification through a central orchestrator, enabling multiple users to collaborate securely through their respective agents.

### [28] [Explicit Trait Inference for Multi-Agent Coordination](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19278v2)
*Suhaib Abdurahman,Etsuko Ishii,Katerina Margatina,Divya Bhargavi,Monica Sunkara,Yi Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent协作中的显式特质推断方法，可显著提升协调效果，可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出显式特质推理（ETI）方法，使LLM智能体从交互历史中推断伙伴的温暖度和能力特质，从而减少协调失败，在实验中显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于LLM的多智能体系统在复杂任务中容易发生协调失败（如目标漂移、错误级联），需要改进协调机制。

Method: ETI方法：智能体从交互历史中推断并跟踪伙伴在温暖度和能力两个心理学维度上的特质，利用这些特质信息指导决策。

Result: 经济博弈中收益损失减少45-77%；MultiAgentBench中性能提升3-29%（取决于场景和模型）；特质配置文件能预测智能体行为，信息丰富的配置文件带来更大改进。

Conclusion: ETI是一种轻量级且稳健的协调改进机制，首次系统性证明LLM智能体能够可靠推断他人特质并利用结构化特质认知进行协调。

中文摘要：基于LLM的多智能体系统（MAS）在复杂任务中展现出潜力，但仍然容易出现协调失败，例如目标漂移、错误级联和错位行为。我们提出了显式特质推理（ETI），一种基于心理学的协调改进方法。ETI使智能体能够从交互历史中推断和跟踪伙伴在两个既定心理学维度——温暖度（如信任）和能力（如技能）——上的特征，以指导决策。我们在受控环境（经济博弈）中评估了ETI，它减少了45-77%的收益损失；在更现实、复杂的多智能体环境（MultiAgentBench）中，相对于CoT基线，根据场景和模型不同，ETI将性能提升了3-29%。额外分析表明，收益与特质推理紧密相关：ETI配置文件预测了智能体的行为，信息丰富的配置文件推动了改进。这些结果突显了ETI作为一种轻量级且稳健的机制，用于改善各种多智能体环境中的协调，并提供了首个系统性证据，证明LLM智能体能够（i）从交互历史中可靠地推断他人特质，以及（ii）利用对他人特质的结构化认知进行协调。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems (MAS) show promise on complex tasks but remain prone to coordination failures such as goal drift, error cascades, and misaligned behaviors. We propose Explicit Trait Inference (ETI), a psychologically grounded method for improving coordination. ETI enables agents to infer and track partner characteristics along two established psychological dimensions--warmth (e.g., trust) and competence (e.g., skill)--from interaction histories to guide decisions. We evaluate ETI in controlled settings (economic games), where it reduces payoff loss by 45-77%, and in more realistic, complex multi-agent settings (MultiAgentBench), where it improves performance by 3-29% depending on the scenario and model, relative to a CoT baseline. Additional analysis shows that gains are closely linked to trait inference: ETI profiles predict agents' actions, and informative profiles drive improvements. These results highlight ETI as a lightweight and robust mechanism for improving coordination in diverse multi-agent settings, and provide the first systematic evidence that LLM agents can (i) reliably infer others' traits from interaction histories and (ii) leverage structured awareness of others' traits for coordination.
