### [80] [Decompose, Structure, and Repair: A Neuro-Symbolic Framework for Autoformalization via Operator Trees](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19000v2)
*Xiaoyang Liu,Zineng Dong,Yifan Bai,Yantao Li,Yuntian Liu,Tao Luo*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 神经符号框架分解修复形式化代码，对代码修复agent有启发

TL;DR: 提出了DSR框架，通过分解、结构和修复将自动形式化重构为模块化流水线，利用算子树进行错误定位和修复，并在新基准PRIME上取得最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将形式代码视为扁平序列，忽略了数学语句的层次逻辑，导致自动形式化效果受限。

Method: DSR框架：将语句分解为逻辑组件，映射为结构化算子树，通过子树精炼定位和修复错误。

Result: 在PRIME基准上，DSR在同等计算预算下持续优于基线，达到新最优性能。

Conclusion: DSR通过利用层次结构有效提升了自动形式化的准确性和鲁棒性，为未来研究提供了新范式。

中文摘要：语句自动形式化是连接人类数学和形式数学的关键桥梁，它将自然语言问题翻译成形式语言。以往的工作侧重于数据合成和多样化的训练范式以优化端到端的大语言模型（LLMs），但它们通常将形式代码视为扁平序列，忽略了数学语句中固有的层次逻辑。在这项工作中，我们引入了DSR（分解、结构和修复），一个神经符号框架，将自动形式化重构为模块化流水线。DSR将语句分解为逻辑组件，并将它们映射到结构化的算子树，利用这一拓扑蓝图通过子树精炼来精确定位和修复错误。此外，我们介绍了PRIME，一个包含156个选自经典教材并经过专家在Lean 4中注释的本科和研究生级定理的基准。实验结果表明，DSR达到了新的最优性能，在同等计算预算下始终优于基线。数据集、模型和代码可在https://github.com/XiaoyangLiu-sjtu/DSR获取。

Original abstract: Statement autoformalization acts as a critical bridge between human mathematics and formal mathematics by translating natural language problems into formal language. While prior works have focused on data synthesis and diverse training paradigms to optimize end-to-end Large Language Models (LLMs), they typically treat formal code as flat sequences, neglecting the hierarchical logic inherent in mathematical statements. In this work, we introduce Decompose, Structure, and Repair (DSR), a neuro-symbolic framework that restructures autoformalization into a modular pipeline. DSR decomposes statements into logical components and maps them to structured operator trees, leveraging this topological blueprint to precisely localize and repair errors via sub-tree refinement. Furthermore, we introduce PRIME, a benchmark of 156 undergraduate and graduate-level theorems selected from canonical textbooks and expertly annotated in Lean 4. Experimental results demonstrate that DSR establishes a new state-of-the-art, consistently outperforming baselines under equivalent computational budgets. The datasets, model, and code are available at https://github.com/XiaoyangLiu-sjtu/DSR.

</details>


### [81] [Evaluation-driven Scaling for Scientific Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19341v1)
*Haotian Ye,Haowei Lin,Jingyi Tang,Yizhen Luo,Caiyin Yang,Chang Su,Rahul Thapa,Rui Yang,Ruihua Liu,Zeyu Li,Chong Gao,Dachao Ding,Guangrong He,Miaolei Zhang,Lina Sun,Wenyang Wang,Yuchen Zhong,Zhuohao Shen,Di He,Jianzhu Ma,Stefano Ermon,Tongyang Li,Xiaowen Chu,James Zou,Yuzhi Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 评估驱动的科学发现框架，含并行探索与反馈优化，且加速了LASSO算法2倍，与自动代码优化直接相关。

TL;DR: 提出SimpleTES框架，通过并行探索、反馈驱动改进和局部选择来扩展评估驱动的发现循环，在21个科学问题上用gpt-oss模型取得最优结果，并具备泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作强调评估重要性但未系统研究如何有效扩展评估驱动的发现循环以推动科学发现边界。

Method: 提出SimpleTES框架，策略性地结合并行探索、反馈驱动改进和局部选择，在测试时通过评估驱动扩展。

Result: 在跨越六个领域的21个科学问题中，SimpleTES使用gpt-oss模型取得最优结果，例如LASSO提速2倍以上、量子电路门开销减少24.5%、Erdos最小重叠构造超越已知最佳；后训练成功轨迹可泛化到未知问题。

Conclusion: 有效的评估驱动循环扩展是推进LLM驱动科学发现的核心，SimpleTES提供了一个简单实用的框架来实现这些收益。

中文摘要：语言模型越来越多地用于科学发现，以生成假设、提出候选解决方案、实现系统并迭代改进它们。这些试错循环的核心是评估：通过验证器、模拟器或特定任务评分函数获取候选解决方案反馈的过程。虽然先前的工作强调了评估的重要性，但尚未明确阐述如何以原则性和有效的方式扩展评估驱动的发现循环，以推动科学发现的边界，这是本文试图解决的问题。我们提出了简单测试时评估驱动扩展（SimpleTES），这是一个通用框架，策略性地结合了并行探索、反馈驱动改进和局部选择，揭示了通过沿正确维度扩展评估驱动的发现循环所解锁的巨大收益。在跨越六个领域的21个科学问题中，SimpleTES使用gpt-oss模型发现了最先进的解决方案，始终优于前沿模型基线和复杂的优化流水线。特别是，我们将广泛使用的LASSO算法加速了2倍以上，设计了量子电路路由策略，将门开销减少了24.5%，并发现了超越已知最佳结果的Erdos最小重叠构造。除了新颖的发现，SimpleTES还产生了轨迹级历史，自然地为反馈驱动学习提供监督。当在成功轨迹上进行后训练时，模型不仅提高了在已知问题上的效率，而且泛化到未知问题，发现了基础模型未能发现的解决方案。总之，我们的结果将有效的评估驱动循环扩展确立为推进LLM驱动的科学发现的核心轴，并提供了一个简单而实用的框架来实现这些收益。

Original abstract: Language models are increasingly used in scientific discovery to generate hypotheses, propose candidate solutions, implement systems, and iteratively refine them. At the core of these trial-and-error loops lies evaluation: the process of obtaining feedback on candidate solutions via verifiers, simulators, or task-specific scoring functions. While prior work has highlighted the importance of evaluation, it has not explicitly formulated the problem of how evaluation-driven discovery loops can be scaled up in a principled and effective manner to push the boundaries of scientific discovery, a problem this paper seeks to address. We introduce Simple Test-time Evaluation-driven Scaling (SimpleTES), a general framework that strategically combines parallel exploration, feedback-driven refinement, and local selection, revealing substantial gains unlocked by scaling evaluation-driven discovery loops along the right dimensions. Across 21 scientific problems spanning six domains, SimpleTES discovers state-of-the-art solutions using gpt-oss models, consistently outperforming both frontier-model baselines and sophisticated optimization pipelines. Particularly, we sped up the widely used LASSO algorithm by over 2x, designed quantum circuit routing policies that reduce gate overhead by 24.5%, and discovered new Erdos minimum overlap constructions that surpass the best-known results. Beyond novel discoveries, SimpleTES produces trajectory-level histories that naturally supervise feedback-driven learning. When post-trained on successful trajectories, models not only improve efficiency on seen problems but also generalize to unseen problems, discovering solutions that base models fail to uncover. Together, our results establish effective evaluation-driven loop scaling as a central axis for advancing LLM-driven scientific discovery, and provide a simple yet practical framework for realizing these gains.

</details>


### [82] [EVPO: Explained Variance Policy Optimization for Adaptive Critic Utilization in LLM Post-Training](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19485v1)
*Chengjun Pan,Shichun Liu,Jiahang Lin,Dingwei Zhu,Jiazheng Zhang,Shihan Dou,Songyang Gao,Zhenhua Han,Binghai Wang,Rui Zheng,Xuanjing Huang,Tao Gui,Yansong Feng*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出自适应基线选择的RL算法EVPO，可适用于agent训练中的方差减少。

TL;DR: 提出EVPO，通过可解释方差在PPO和GRPO之间自适应切换，在稀疏奖励设置中优于两者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典RL后训练中，使用评论家基线（如PPO）在稀疏奖励下可能引入噪声增大方差，而无评论家方法（如GRPO）虽简单但性能有局限，需要一种能自动选择更优基线的方法。

Method: 将基线选择建模为卡尔曼滤波，利用可解释方差（EV）判断评论家是否降低方差，提出EVPO在每个训练步骤根据批次EV自适应切换评论家或批次均值基线。

Result: 在经典控制、智能体交互和数学推理四项任务上，EVPO始终优于PPO和GRPO，无论哪个固定基线更强，且自适应门控机制有效跟踪评论家成熟度，零阈值经验最优。

Conclusion: EVPO通过自适应基线选择，结合评论家和无评论家方法的优点，在稀疏奖励下显著提升RL后训练性能，具有理论保障和实证有效性。

中文摘要：针对大语言模型后训练中的强化学习（RL）面临一个基本设计选择：是否使用学习到的评论家（critic）作为策略优化的基线。经典理论倾向于使用基于评论家的方法（如PPO）以降低方差，但无评论家替代方法（如GRPO）因其简单性和竞争性能而得到广泛应用。我们证明，在稀疏奖励设置中，学习到的评论家可能会注入超出其捕获状态信号的估计噪声，从而增加而非减少优势函数的方差。通过将基线选择视为卡尔曼滤波问题，我们将PPO和GRPO统一为卡尔曼增益的两个极端，并证明从单个训练批次即可计算的可解释方差（EV）能够识别精确边界：正EV表示评论家降低方差，而零或负EV则表示评论家增加方差。基于这一见解，我们提出可解释方差策略优化（EVPO），该方法监控每个训练步骤的批次级EV，并在基于评论家和批次均值优势估计之间自适应切换，理论上保证每步的方差不超过两者中更好的一个。在涵盖经典控制、智能体交互和数学推理的四项任务中，无论给定任务上哪个固定基线更强，EVPO始终优于PPO和GRPO。进一步分析证实，自适应门控机制能够跟踪训练过程中评论家成熟度的变化，并且理论推导的零阈值在经验上是最优的。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) for LLM post-training faces a fundamental design choice: whether to use a learned critic as a baseline for policy optimization. Classical theory favors critic-based methods such as PPO for variance reduction, yet critic-free alternatives like GRPO have gained widespread adoption due to their simplicity and competitive performance. We show that in sparse-reward settings, a learned critic can inject estimation noise that exceeds the state signal it captures, increasing rather than reducing advantage variance. By casting baseline selection as a Kalman filtering problem, we unify PPO and GRPO as two extremes of the Kalman gain and prove that explained variance (EV), computable from a single training batch, identifies the exact boundary: positive EV indicates the critic reduces variance, while zero or negative EV signals that it inflates variance. Building on this insight, we propose Explained Variance Policy Optimization (EVPO), which monitors batch-level EV at each training step and adaptively switches between critic-based and batch-mean advantage estimation, provably achieving no greater variance than the better of the two at every step. Across four tasks spanning classical control, agentic interaction, and mathematical reasoning, EVPO consistently outperforms both PPO and GRPO regardless of which fixed baseline is stronger on a given task. Further analysis confirms that the adaptive gating tracks critic maturation over training and that the theoretically derived zero threshold is empirically optimal.

</details>


### [83] [FASTER: Value-Guided Sampling for Fast RL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19730v1)
*Perry Dong,Alexander Swerdlow,Dorsa Sadigh,Chelsea Finn*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于价值引导的采样加速RL，涉及测试时缩放，可迁移到agent推理时采样优化。

TL;DR: 提出FASTER方法，通过将动作去噪过程建模为MDP来高效实现测试时扩展，降低计算成本并提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于采样的测试时扩展方法计算成本高，旨在不增加计算负担的情况下获得性能提升。

Method: 将多个动作候选的去噪和选择建模为MDP，在去噪空间中学习策略和值函数以预测动作价值并逐步过滤低价值候选。

Result: 在长程操作任务上一致改进基础策略，达到最佳性能；应用于预训练VLA时保持性能的同时大幅降低计算需求。

Conclusion: FASTER是一种轻量级、可插拔的方法，能有效提升生成式强化学习算法的效率。

中文摘要：一些目前性能最强的强化学习算法由于使用了测试时扩展方法（例如采样多个动作候选并选择最佳的一个）而变得极其昂贵。在这项工作中，我们提出了FASTER，一种通过将动作样本的性能增益追溯到去噪过程早期来获得基于采样的测试时扩展带来的好处而无需计算成本的方法。我们的关键洞察是，我们可以将多个动作候选的去噪和选择最佳动作建模为一个马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），其目标是在去噪完成前逐步过滤动作候选。通过这个MDP，我们可以在去噪空间中学习一个策略和值函数，用于预测去噪过程中动作候选的下游价值，并在最大化回报的同时对其进行过滤。结果是一种轻量级的方法，可以插入到现有的生成式强化学习算法中。在在线和批量在线强化学习中的挑战性长程操作任务中，FASTER一致地改进了基础策略，并在比较方法中实现了最佳的整体性能。应用于预训练的VLA时，FASTER在显著降低训练和推理计算需求的同时实现了相同的性能。代码可在https://github.com/alexanderswerdlow/faster获取。

Original abstract: Some of the most performant reinforcement learning algorithms today can be prohibitively expensive as they use test-time scaling methods such as sampling multiple action candidates and selecting the best one. In this work, we propose FASTER, a method for getting the benefits of sampling-based test-time scaling of diffusion-based policies without the computational cost by tracing the performance gain of action samples back to earlier in the denoising process. Our key insight is that we can model the denoising of multiple action candidates and selecting the best one as a Markov Decision Process (MDP) where the goal is to progressively filter action candidates before denoising is complete. With this MDP, we can learn a policy and value function in the denoising space that predicts the downstream value of action candidates in the denoising process and filters them while maximizing returns. The result is a method that is lightweight and can be plugged into existing generative RL algorithms. Across challenging long-horizon manipulation tasks in online and batch-online RL, FASTER consistently improves the underlying policies and achieves the best overall performance among the compared methods. Applied to a pretrained VLA, FASTER achieves the same performance while substantially reducing training and inference compute requirements. Code is available at https://github.com/alexanderswerdlow/faster .

</details>


### [84] [DR-Venus: Towards Frontier Edge-Scale Deep Research Agents with Only 10K Open Data](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19859v1)
*Venus Team,Sunhao Dai,Yong Deng,Jinzhen Lin,Yusheng Song,Guoqing Wang,Xiaofeng Wu,Yuqi Zhou,Shuo Yang,Zhenzhe Ying,Zhanwei Zhang,Changhua Meng,Weiqiang Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 边缘深度研究agent训练，使用SFT和RL改进长程任务执行，直接相关于coding agent训练。

TL;DR: DR-Venus是一个基于小语言模型的4B参数深度研究智能体，通过改进数据质量和利用率的训练方法，在开放数据下显著优于同类小模型，并缩小了与更大模型的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在实际部署中利用小语言模型在成本、延迟和隐私方面的优势，研究如何在有限的开放数据下训练强大的小型深度研究智能体。

Method: 采用两阶段训练：第一阶段使用代理监督微调（SFT）结合数据清洗和长程轨迹重采样；第二阶段应用基于IGPO的代理强化学习（RL），设计基于信息增益和格式感知正则化的回合级奖励。

Result: DR-Venus-4B在多个深度研究基准上显著优于9B参数以下的代理模型，并缩小了与30B类系统的差距。

Conclusion: 小模型（4B参数）具备强大的性能潜力，验证了其部署前景和测试时缩放的价值；公开模型、代码和方案以促进可复现研究。

中文摘要：基于小语言模型的边缘规模深度研究智能体因其在成本、延迟和隐私方面的优势，对于实际部署具有吸引力。在这项工作中，我们研究如何通过提高数据质量和数据利用率，在有限的开放数据下训练一个强大的小型深度研究智能体。我们提出了DR-Venus，一个前沿的4B深度研究智能体，用于边缘规模部署，完全基于开放数据构建。我们的训练方案包括两个阶段。在第一阶段，我们使用代理监督微调（SFT）来建立基本的代理能力，结合严格的数据清洗和对长程轨迹的重新采样，以提高数据质量和利用率。在第二阶段，我们应用代理强化学习（RL）来进一步提高长程深度研究任务上的执行可靠性。为了使RL在此设置中对小智能体有效，我们基于IGPO设计了基于信息增益和格式感知正则化的回合级奖励，从而增强了监督密度和回合级信用分配。完全基于大约10K开放数据，DR-Venus-4B在多个深度研究基准上显著优于之前9B参数以下的代理模型，同时缩小了与更大规模30B类系统的差距。我们的进一步分析表明，4B智能体已经具备惊人的强大性能潜力，突显了小模型的部署前景以及在此设置中测试时缩放的价值。我们发布了我们的模型、代码和关键方案，以支持边缘规模深度研究智能体的可复现研究。

Original abstract: Edge-scale deep research agents based on small language models are attractive for real-world deployment due to their advantages in cost, latency, and privacy. In this work, we study how to train a strong small deep research agent under limited open-data by improving both data quality and data utilization. We present DR-Venus, a frontier 4B deep research agent for edge-scale deployment, built entirely on open data. Our training recipe consists of two stages. In the first stage, we use agentic supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to establish basic agentic capability, combining strict data cleaning with resampling of long-horizon trajectories to improve data quality and utilization. In the second stage, we apply agentic reinforcement learning (RL) to further improve execution reliability on long-horizon deep research tasks. To make RL effective for small agents in this setting, we build on IGPO and design turn-level rewards based on information gain and format-aware regularization, thereby enhancing supervision density and turn-level credit assignment. Built entirely on roughly 10K open-data, DR-Venus-4B significantly outperforms prior agentic models under 9B parameters on multiple deep research benchmarks, while also narrowing the gap to much larger 30B-class systems. Our further analysis shows that 4B agents already possess surprisingly strong performance potential, highlighting both the deployment promise of small models and the value of test-time scaling in this setting. We release our models, code, and key recipes to support reproducible research on edge-scale deep research agents.

### [85] [Reinforcing privacy reasoning in LLMs via normative simulacra from fiction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20904v1)
*Matt Franchi,Madiha Zahrah Choksi,Harold Triedman,Helen Nissenbaum*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 通过RL训练LLM进行隐私推理，使用GRPO和奖励工程，可迁移至agent安全控制。

TL;DR: 从小说中提取规范模拟，通过监督学习和GRPO强化学习微调LLM，使其学会情境隐私推理，并在多个基准上取得最佳性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理的隐私处理与用户期望不一致，且现有方法成本高或泛化差，需要一种低成本、可泛化的情境隐私推理方法。

Method: 从小说中提取规范模拟，用监督学习（SFT）和GRPO强化学习微调LLM，奖励函数结合程序化信号和LLM裁判，并引入对比评分防止过拟合。

Result: SFT提高隐私识别但非判断正确性；GRPO+规范基础在法律合规基准得分最高，且与人类隐私期望相关性最强，证明小说训练的隐私推理可迁移到现实领域。

Conclusion: 小说衍生的规范模拟能有效教会LLM情境隐私推理，且跨域迁移表现良好，为隐私对齐提供了新途径。

中文摘要：LLM代理的信息处理实践与用户的情境隐私期望广泛不一致。情境完整性（CI）提供了一个原则性框架，将隐私定义为信息在情境相关规范内的适当流动。然而，现有方法要么通过监督者-助手架构使推理成本加倍，要么在狭窄的任务特定数据上微调。我们提出从小说中提取规范模拟（规范和信息流的结构化表示），并通过监督学习后接GRPO强化学习来微调LLM。我们的复合奖励函数结合了程序化信号，包括任务清晰度（包含模式有效性、构造区分和提取置信度）、结构完整性、内部一致性和情境识别，以及一个LLM裁判，评估模型的隐私推理是否基于源文本的保留规范宇宙。为了缓解过拟合，我们引入了每次完成的对比评分：每个完成既针对正确的规范宇宙，也针对随机选择的错误宇宙进行评估，训练模型根据情境进行条件化，而不是记忆特定源的规范。我们在五个涵盖不同社会情境的CI对齐基准上进行了评估，并消融了RL和规范基础的贡献。在七个模型中，SFT引入了限制信息流的保守先验，提高了对隐私相关情境的识别，但未提高隐私判断的正确性。带有规范基础的GRPO在法律合规基准上取得了最高分，并且与人群众包的人类隐私期望相关性最强，表明源自小说的规范模拟可以教授转移到现实世界领域的情境隐私推理。

Original abstract: Information handling practices of LLM agents are broadly misaligned with the contextual privacy expectations of their users. Contextual Integrity (CI) provides a principled framework, defining privacy as the appropriate flow of information within context-relative norms. However, existing approaches either double inference cost via supervisor-assistant architectures, or fine-tune on narrow task-specific data. We propose extracting normative simulacra (structured representations of norms and information flows) from fiction novels and using them to fine-tune LLMs via supervised learning followed by GRPO reinforcement learning. Our composite reward function combines programmatic signals, including task clarity (subsuming schema validity, construct discrimination, and extraction confidence), structural completeness, internal consistency, and context identification, with an LLM judge that evaluates whether the model's privacy reasoning is grounded in the held-out normative universe of the source text. To mitigate overfitting, we introduce per-completion contrastive scoring: each completion is evaluated against both the correct normative universe and a randomly selected wrong one, teaching the model to condition on context rather than memorize source-specific norms. We evaluate on five CI-aligned benchmarks spanning distinct societal contexts and ablate the contributions of RL and normative grounding. Across seven models, SFT introduces a conservative prior toward restricting information flow, improving recognition of privacy-relevant situations but not the correctness of privacy judgments. GRPO with normative grounding achieves the highest score on a law compliance benchmark and strongest correlation with crowdsourced human privacy expectations, demonstrating that fiction-derived normative simulacra can teach contextual privacy reasoning that transfers to real-world domains.

### [86] [MoBayes: A Modular Bayesian Framework for Separating Reasoning from Language in Conversational Clinical Decision Support](http://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20022v3)
*Yusuf Kesmen,Fay Elhassan,Jiayi Ma,Julien Stalhandske,Yena Chang,David Sasu,Alexandra Kulinkina,Akhil Arora,Lars Klein,Mary-Anne Hartley*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: MoBayes框架分离推理与语言生成，模块化agent架构，可迁移至可靠决策agent。

TL;DR: MoBayes通过分离推理与语言生成，在临床对话中实现了更好的决策性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决LLMs在临床决策中混淆概率推理和语言生成的架构局限性。

Method: 提出MoBayes框架，LLM仅作为语言接口，贝叶斯模块进行概率推理、更新后验、选择问题并决定停止或推迟。

Result: MoBayes在各种场景下优于独立LLM医生，且低成本模型搭配MoBayes可超越更大模型。

Conclusion: 可靠的临床决策支持应分离推理与语言生成，而非仅扩大模型规模。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地用于对话式临床决策支持，然而它们将下一个令牌预测与概率决策混为一谈。我们认为这种混淆反映了一个架构上的局限性：此类系统缺乏明确的后验跟踪、可控的弃权阈值和可审计的推理链。我们引入了MoBayes，一个模块化贝叶斯对话框架，它将推理与语言分离。LLM仅作为语言接口，将患者对话解析为结构化观察，而贝叶斯模块对这些观察进行概率推理以更新后验，通过期望信息增益选择后续问题，并通过校准的决策阈值决定何时停止或推迟。这种设计实现了明确的后验跟踪、可控的选择性决策以及无需重新训练语言模型即可替换的群体特定统计后端。在经验知识和LLM生成的知识库上，MoBayes的表现优于独立的顶尖LLM医生，包括匹配模型族的比较，其中廉价的传感器模型与MoBayes配对，以更低的成本超过了更大的自主模型。这一优势在面对对抗性患者沟通风格和不同诊断场景时仍然存在。这些结果表明，可靠的对话式临床决策支持系统应将概率推理与语言生成分离，而非仅仅扩大模型规模。代码可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/MoBayes/获取。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used for conversational clinical decision support, yet they conflate next token prediction with probabilistic decision making. We argue that this conflation reflects an architectural limitation: such systems lack explicit posterior tracking, controllable abstention thresholds, and auditable reasoning chains. We introduce MoBayes, a Modular Bayesian dialogue framework that separates reasoning from language. The LLM acts only as a language interface, parsing patient conversation into structured observations, while a Bayesian module performs probabilistic inference over these observations to update posteriors, select follow-up questions via expected-information-gain and determine when to stop or defer through calibrated decision thresholds. This design enables explicit posterior tracking, controllable selective decision-making, and replaceable population-specific statistical backends without retraining the language model. Across empirical and LLM-generated knowledge bases, MoBayes outperforms standalone frontier LLM doctors, including matched model-family comparisons where inexpensive sensor models paired with MoBayes exceed larger autonomous models at lower cost. The advantage persists under adversarial patient communication styles and across varying diagnostic scenarios. These results suggest that reliable conversational clinical decision support systems should separate probabilistic reasoning from language generation rather than scaling model size alone. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/MoBayes/

</details>
